User has answered your questions: "verify-path.html に以下の機能を追加し、インタラクティブに制御点を調整できるようにする方針でどうでしょうか？

1. Douglas-Peucker アルゴリズムで自動間引き（許容誤差スライダーで点数を調整）
2. 間引いた制御点間を Catmull-Rom スプライン補間（制御点が曲線上に乗るので直感的）
3. 制御点をドラッグで移動できるエディタ機能
4. 編集結果をJSONエクスポートして cat-path.json に保存

つまり verify-path.html を「パスエディタ」に進化させて、そこで最終的なパスを確定する流れです。"="この方針でOK（推奨）". You can now continue with the user's answers in mind.

## Approved Plan:
# ねこえがく：LUT方式から静的パス+数式近似方式への移行計画

## Context

現在のアーキテクチャは、ゲーム開始時に手描き画像（head.png + tail.png）からピクセルスキャンで輪郭を抽出し、LUT（ルックアップテーブル）を構築する方式。これを廃止し、**正解のねこのパスを静的データとして事前定義**し、**セグメントごとに数式で近似**する方式に一新する。

**動機:** 画像解析の環境依存性を排除し、正解パスを完全に制御可能にする。将来の差し替えも容易になる。

**方針決定事項:**
- ゲーム中の正解表示は**手描き画像を継続**（見た目は変わらない）
- 新コードは**game.js に統合**（ファイル分離しない）
- スライダー設計はパスデータ確定後に決定

---

## Step 1: パスエディタの構築とパス確定

**目的:** `tools/verify-path.html` をインタラクティブなパスエディタに進化させ、ユーザーが制御点を調整して正解パスを確定する。

**作業:**
1. `tools/verify-path.html` に以下の機能を追加:
   - **Douglas-Peucker 間引き**: 許容誤差スライダーで点数を調整（~375点 → ~20-50点）
   - **Catmull-Rom スプライン補間**: 間引いた制御点間を滑らかな曲線で繋ぐ（制御点が曲線上に乗る）
   - **ドラッグ編集**: 制御点をマウスドラッグで移動
   - **JSONエクスポート**: 編集結果を `cat-path.json` 形式で出力

2. ユーザーが以下のワークフローでパスを確定:
   - 許容誤差スライダーで適切な点数を探る
   - 元画像とスプライン曲線を重ね合わせ確認
   - ずれている制御点をドラッグで修正
   - 満足したらエクスポート → `config/cat-path.json` に保存

**対象ファイル:** `tools/verify-path.html`（既存を改修）, `config/cat-path.json`（エクスポート結果で上書き）

---

## Step 2: 新しい曲線計算関数を実装

**目的:** `cat-path.json` のセグメント定義に基づき、各数式タイプの計算関数を実装。

**作業:**
1. 各数式タイプの評価関数を実装:
   - `evalCubicBezier(t, p0, p1, p2, p3)` → Y座標
   - `evalQuadBezier(t, p0, p1, p2)` → Y座標
   - `evalGaussian(x, center, amplitude, sigma)` → 寄与量
   - `evalSine(t, amplitude, freq, phase)` → 寄与量
   - `evalSmoothstep(t, height)` → 寄与量
   - `evalLine(t, y0, y1)` → Y座標
2. `getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H)` を書き換え: LUT参照 → セグメント評価
3. `getBottomY(xRatio, params, W, H)` を書き換え: LUT参照 → セグメント評価

**対象ファイル:** `js/game.js`

---

## Step 3: 描画・スコア計算の更新

**作業:**
1. `drawCat()` のストローク描画を新しいセグメント定義に合わせて調整
2. `calculateScore()` を書き換え:
   - 画像参照（refTopY/refBottomY）を廃止
   - answerParamsでの数式評価 vs playerでの数式評価のRMSE比較に変更
   - スライダー影響があるセグメント（ears, tail, feet）のみをスコア対象
3. `init()` から `extractContours()` / `buildBaselineLUT()` の呼び出しを削除し、`cat-path.json` のロードを追加

**対象ファイル:** `js/game.js`, `index.html`（cat-path.jsonのロード追加は不要、loadConfig的な方法で読む）

---

## Step 4: 不要コードの削除と設定整理

**削除する関数・変数:**
- `extractContours()` — 画像ピクセルスキャン
- `buildBaselineLUT()` — LUT構築
- `interpolateBaseline()` — LUT補間
- `smoothContour()` — 輪郭スムージング
- `autoFit()` — 自動フィッティング（グリッドサーチ）
- `getTopYNoEars()`, `getSingleEarContribution()` — ヘルパー
- `refTopY`, `refBottomY`, `refTopBaseline`, `refBottomBaseline` — グローバル変数

**修正する関数:**
- `getEarContribution()` → 新しいガウシアン評価に統合
- `getTailContribution()` → 新しいsmoothstep評価に統合
- `getFeetContribution()` → 新しいsin波評価に統合
- `debugFit()` / `debugSetAnswer()` → 新エンジンベースに書き換え

**残す関数（変更なし）:**
- `loadConfig()`, `loadLang()`, `applyLabels()`, `loadImages()`
- `drawTargetImage()` — 手描き画像の表示は継続
- `drawGrid()`, `drawJunctionPoints()`
- スライダー関連: `resetPlayer()`, `syncSlidersFromPlayer()`, `syncPlayerFromSliders()`, `setupSliderEvents()`
- ゲームフロー: `showScreen()`, `startGame()`, `finishGame()`, `backToTitle()`, `updateTimerDisplay()`
- `renderGame()`, `renderTitle()`, `renderResult()` — 呼び出す関数が変わるだけで構造は同じ
- `getScoreComment()`

**settings.json の整理:**
- `answerParams` → `cat-path.json` に移動
- `strokeBounds`, `strokeJunctions` → `cat-path.json` に統合
- `topLine`, `bottomLine` → 不要になれば削除

**対象ファイル:** `js/game.js`, `config/settings.json`

---

## 検証方法

1. **Step 1 完了後:** ブラウザコンソールで `debugFit()` を実行し、静的パスの曲線と元画像が概ね一致することを目視確認
2. **Step 2 完了後:** スライダーを動かし、耳・しっぽ・足の変形が正しく反映されることを確認
3. **Step 3 完了後:** answerParamsをスライダーに設定して100点が出ることを確認。中間パラメータでスコアの妥当性を確認
4. **Step 4 完了後:** ゲーム全体のフロー（タイトル→ゲーム→結果→もういちど）を一通りテスト
```

    42→
    43→<div class="row">
    44→  <div class="panel" style="flex:1">
    45→    <h2>輪郭データ (抽出結果)</h2>
    46→    <textarea id="contour-data" readonly></textarea>
    47→  </div>
    48→  <div class="panel" style="flex:1">
    49→    <h2>誤差情報</h2>
    50→    <textarea id="error-info" readonly></textarea>
    51→  </div>
    52→</div>
    53→
    54→<script>
    55→const W = 800, H = 400;
    56→const canvas = document.getElementById('cv');
    57→const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    58→
    59→const headImg = new Image();
    60→const tailImg = new Image();
    61→let imagesLoaded = false;
    62→let catPath = null;
    63→
    64→// 抽出された輪郭
    65→let extractedTop = [];  // [{x, y}, ...]
    66→let extractedBottom = [];
    67→
    68→// ---- 画像読み込み ----
    69→function loadImages() {
    70→  return new Promise(resolve => {
    71→    let loaded = 0;
    72→    const onLoad = () => { if (++loaded === 2) { imagesLoaded = true; resolve(); } };
    73→    headImg.src = '../img/head.png';
    74→    tailImg.src = '../img/tail.png';
    75→    headImg.onload = onLoad;
    76→    tailImg.onload = onLoad;
    77→  });
    78→}
    79→
    80→// ---- cat-path.json 読み込み ----
    81→async function loadCatPath() {
    82→  const res = await fetch('../config/cat-path.json');
    83→  catPath = await res.json();
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ---- 画像から輪郭を抽出 ----
    87→function extractContours() {
    88→  const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');
    89→  offscreen.width = W;
    90→  offscreen.height = H;
    91→  const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');
    92→  octx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);
    93→  octx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);
    94→
    95→  const imageData = octx.getImageData(0, 0, W, H);
    96→  const pixels = imageData.data;
    97→  const threshold = 128;
    98→  const step = 2;
    99→
   100→  extractedTop = [];
   101→  extractedBottom = [];
   102→
   103→  for (let px = 0; px < W; px += step) {
   104→    let topOuter = -1, topInner = -1;
   105→    let bottomOuter = -1, bottomInner = -1;
   106→
   107→    // 上の線
   108→    for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {
   109→      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {
   110→        topOuter = y;
   111→        for (let y2 = y + 1; y2 < H; y2++) {
   112→          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) {
   113→            topInner = y2 - 1;
   114→            break;
   115→          }
   116→        }
   117→        if (topInner === -1) topInner = topOuter;
   118→        break;
   119→      }
   120→    }
   121→
   122→    // 下の線
   123→    for (let y = H - 1; y >= 0; y--) {
   124→      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {
   125→        bottomOuter = y;
   126→        for (let y2 = y - 1; y2 >= 0; y2--) {
   127→          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) {
   128→            bottomInner = y2 + 1;
   129→            break;
   130→          }
   131→        }
   132→        if (bottomInner === -1) bottomInner = bottomOuter;
   133→        break;
   134→      }
   135→    }
   136→
   137→    if (topOuter !== -1) {
   138→      extractedTop.push({ x: px / W, y: ((topOuter + topInner) / 2) / H });
   139→    }
   140→    if (bottomOuter !== -1) {
   141→      extractedBottom.push({ x: px / W, y: ((bottomOuter + bottomInner) / 2) / H });
   142→    }
   143→  }
   144→
   145→  // 簡易スムージング
   146→  smoothPoints(extractedTop, 3);
   147→  smoothPoints(extractedBottom, 3);
   148→}
   149→
   150→function smoothPoints(pts, radius) {
   151→  const orig = pts.map(p => p.y);
   152→  for (let i = radius; i < pts.length - radius; i++) {
   153→    let sum = 0;
   154→    for (let j = -radius; j <= radius; j++) sum += orig[i + j];
   155→    pts[i].y = sum / (radius * 2 + 1);
   156→  }
   157→}
   158→
   159→// ---- パスからY座標を計算 ----
   160→function interpolatePath(points, xRatio) {
   161→  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;
   162→  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;
   163→  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;
   164→
   165→  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
   166→    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) {
   167→      const t = (xRatio - points[i].x) / (points[i + 1].x - points[i].x);
   168→      return points[i].y + t * (points[i + 1].y - points[i].y);
   169→    }
   170→  }
   171→  return null;
   172→}
   173→
   174→// ---- 描画 ----
   175→function draw() {
   176→  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
   177→
   178→  const showImage = document.getElementById('chk-image').checked;
   179→  const showContour = document.getElementById('chk-contour').checked;
   180→  const showPath = document.getElementById('chk-path').checked;
   181→
   182→  const showGrid = document.getElementById('chk-grid').checked;
   183→  const showPoints = document.getElementById('chk-points').checked;
   184→
   185→  // グリッド
   186→  if (showGrid) {
   187→    ctx.strokeStyle = '#eee';
   188→    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
   189→    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 40) {
   190→      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, 0); ctx.lineTo(x, H); ctx.stroke();
   191→    }
   192→    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) {
   193→      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, y); ctx.lineTo(W, y); ctx.stroke();
   194→    }
   195→    // 座標目盛
   196→    ctx.fillStyle = '#aaa';
   197→    ctx.font = '9px monospace';
   198→    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 80) {
   199→      ctx.fillText((x / W).toFixed(2), x + 2, 10);
   200→    }
   201→    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) {
   202→      ctx.fillText((y / H).toFixed(2), 2, y + 10);
   203→    }
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  // 元画像
   207→  if (showImage && imagesLoaded) {
   208→    ctx.save();
   209→    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.25;
   210→    ctx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);
   211→    ctx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);
   212→    ctx.restore();
   213→  }
   214→
   215→  // 抽出輪郭
   216→  if (showContour) {
   217→    drawPolyline(extractedTop, '#ff0000', 1.5);
   218→    drawPolyline(extractedBottom, '#0000ff', 1.5);
   219→  }
   220→
   221→  // 定義パス
   222→  if (catPath && showPath) {
   223→    if (catPath.topLine) {
   224→      drawDefinedLine(catPath.topLine, '#00cc00', 2);
   225→    }
   226→    if (catPath.bottomLine) {
   227→      drawDefinedLine(catPath.bottomLine, '#ff8800', 2);
   228→    }
   229→  }
   230→
   231→  // 制御点
   232→  if (showPoints && catPath) {
   233→    const allPoints = [
   234→      ...(catPath.topLine || []),
   235→      ...(catPath.bottomLine || [])
   236→    ];
   237→    for (const p of allPoints) {
   238→      ctx.fillStyle = '#00cc00';
   239→      ctx.beginPath();
   240→      ctx.arc(p.x * W, p.y * H, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
   241→      ctx.fill();
   242→      ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
   243→      ctx.font = '9px monospace';
   244→      ctx.fillText(`(${p.x.toFixed(3)}, ${p.y.toFixed(3)})`, p.x * W + 6, p.y * H - 6);
   245→    }
   246→  }
   247→
   248→  // 誤差計算
   249→  if (catPath) {
   250→    computeErrors();
   251→  }
   252→}
   253→
   254→function drawPolyline(points, color, width) {
   255→  if (points.length < 2) return;
   256→  ctx.strokeStyle = color;
   257→  ctx.lineWidth = width;
   258→  ctx.beginPath();
   259→  ctx.moveTo(points[0].x * W, points[0].y * H);
   260→  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) {
   261→    ctx.lineTo(points[i].x * W, points[i].y * H);
   262→  }
   263→  ctx.stroke();
   264→}
   265→
   266→function drawDefinedLine(points, color, width) {
   267→  if (points.length < 2) return;
   268→  ctx.strokeStyle = color;
   269→  ctx.lineWidth = width;
   270→  ctx.beginPath();
   271→  ctx.moveTo(points[0].x * W, points[0].y * H);
   272→  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) {
   273→    ctx.lineTo(points[i].x * W, points[i].y * H);
   274→  }
   275→  ctx.stroke();
   276→}
   277→
   278→// ---- 誤差計算 ----
   279→function computeErrors() {
   280→  if (!catPath || !extractedTop.length) return;
   281→
   282→  const lines = [];
   283→  let topErr = 0, topCount = 0;
   284→  let botErr = 0, botCount = 0;
   285→
   286→  for (const pt of extractedTop) {
   287→    const pathY = interpolatePath(catPath.topLine, pt.x);
   288→    if (pathY !== null) {
   289→      const diff = (pt.y - pathY) * H;
   290→      topErr += diff * diff;
   291→      topCount++;
   292→    }
   293→  }
   294→
   295→  for (const pt of extractedBottom) {
   296→    const pathY = interpolatePath(catPath.bottomLine, pt.x);
   297→    if (pathY !== null) {
   298→      const diff = (pt.y - pathY) * H;
   299→      botErr += diff * diff;
   300→      botCount++;
   301→    }
   302→  }
   303→
   304→  const topRmse = topCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(topErr / topCount) : 0;
   305→  const botRmse = botCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(botErr / botCount) : 0;
   306→
   307→  lines.push(`上の線 RMSE: ${topRmse.toFixed(2)} px (${topCount} samples)`);
   308→  lines.push(`下の線 RMSE: ${botRmse.toFixed(2)} px (${botCount} samples)`);
   309→  lines.push(`合計 RMSE: ${Math.sqrt((topErr + botErr) / (topCount + botCount)).toFixed(2)} px`);
   310→  lines.push('');
   311→  lines.push('--- セグメント別誤差 ---');
   312→
   313→  // セグメント別
   314→  const segments = [
   315→    { name: '顔(上)', start: 0.0, end: 0.07, data: extractedTop, baseline: catPath.topLine },
   316→    { name: '耳', start: 0.07, end: 0.305, data: extractedTop, baseline: catPath.topLine },
   317→    { name: '背中', start: 0.305, end: 0.88, data: extractedTop, baseline: catPath.topLine },
   318→    { name: 'しっぽ(上)', start: 0.88, end: 1.0, data: extractedTop, baseline: catPath.topLine },
   319→    { name: '顔(下)', start: 0.0, end: 0.155, data: extractedBottom, baseline: catPath.bottomLine },
   320→    { name: 'あご→足', start: 0.155, end: 0.20, data: extractedBottom, baseline: catPath.bottomLine },
   321→    { name: '足', start: 0.20, end: 0.91, data: extractedBottom, baseline: catPath.bottomLine },
   322→    { name: 'お尻', start: 0.91, end: 1.0, data: extractedBottom, baseline: catPath.bottomLine },
   323→  ];
   324→
   325→  for (const seg of segments) {
   326→    let err = 0, cnt = 0;
   327→    for (const pt of seg.data) {
   328→      if (pt.x < seg.start || pt.x > seg.end) continue;
   329→      const pathY = interpolatePath(seg.baseline, pt.x);
   330→      if (pathY !== null) {
   331→        const diff = (pt.y - pathY) * H;
   332→        err += diff * diff;
   333→        cnt++;
   334→      }
   335→    }
   336→    const rmse = cnt > 0 ? Math.sqrt(err / cnt) : 0;
   337→    lines.push(`  ${seg.name}: RMSE=${rmse.toFixed(2)}px (${cnt} samples)`);
   338→  }
   339→
   340→  document.getElementById('error-info').value = lines.join('\n');
   341→}
   342→
   343→// ---- 輪郭データエクスポート ----
   344→function exportContour() {
   345→  const data = {
   346→    top: extractedTop.map(p => ({ x: +p.x.toFixed(4), y: +p.y.toFixed(4) })),
   347→    bottom: extractedBottom.map(p => ({ x: +p.x.toFixed(4), y: +p.y.toFixed(4) }))
   348→  };
   349→  document.getElementById('contour-data').value = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
   350→}
   351→
   352→// ---- チェックボックスイベント ----
   353→document.querySelectorAll('input[type=checkbox]').forEach(el => {
   354→  el.addEventListener('change', draw);
   355→});
   356→
   357→// ---- 初期化 ----
   358→async function init() {
   359→  await Promise.all([loadImages(), loadCatPath()]);
   360→  extractContours();
   361→  exportContour();
   362→  draw();
   363→}
   364→
   365→init();
   366→</script>
   367→</body>
   368→</html>
   369→
```

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:05:09.129Z)*

*🔧 ツール実行: `Write`*
```
{
  "file_path": "c:\\dev\\nekoegaku\\tools\\verify-path.html",
  "content": "<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang=\"ja\">\n<head>\n<meta charset=\"UTF-8\">\n<title>ねこパスエディタ</title>\n<style>\n  * { box-sizing: border-box; }\n  body { margin: 20px; font-family: monospace; background: #f5f5f5; }\n  h2 { margin: 10px 0 5px; }\n  canvas { border: 1px solid #999; background: #fff; display: block; margin: 10px 0; cursor: crosshair; }\n  .row { display: flex; gap: 20px; flex-wrap: wrap; }\n  .panel { background: #fff; padding: 15px; border: 1px solid #ddd; border-radius: 4px; margin-bottom: 10px; }\n  label { display: inline-block; margin: 2px 8px; font-size: 13px; }\n  textarea { width: 100%; height: 250px; font-size: 11px; font-family: monospace; }\n  button { margin: 5px; padding: 6px 16px; cursor: pointer; }\n  button.primary { background: #2ecc71; color: #fff; border: none; font-weight: bold; }\n  .legend { font-size: 12px; margin: 5px 0; }\n  .legend span { display: inline-block; width: 30px; height: 3px; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 5px; }\n  .slider-row { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px; margin: 5px 0; }\n  .slider-row input[type=range] { flex: 1; }\n  .slider-row .val { min-width: 80px; font-size: 12px; }\n  .info { font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin: 3px 0; }\n  .status { font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: bold; margin: 5px 0; }\n</style>\n</head>\n<body>\n<h1>ねこパスエディタ</h1>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>表示</h2>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-image\" checked> 元画像</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-contour\" checked> 抽出輪郭</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-spline\" checked> スプライン曲線</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-points\" checked> 制御点</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-grid\"> グリッド</label>\n\n  <div class=\"legend\">\n    <span style=\"background:#ff0000\"></span>抽出輪郭(上)\n    <span style=\"background:#0000ff\"></span>抽出輪郭(下)\n    <span style=\"background:#00cc00\"></span>スプライン(上)\n    <span style=\"background:#ff8800\"></span>スプライン(下)\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>間引き (Douglas-Peucker)</h2>\n  <div class=\"slider-row\">\n    <label>上の線 許容誤差:</label>\n    <input type=\"range\" id=\"sl-tol-top\" min=\"0.1\" max=\"20\" step=\"0.1\" value=\"3\">\n    <span class=\"val\" id=\"val-tol-top\">3.0px</span>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"slider-row\">\n    <label>下の線 許容誤差:</label>\n    <input type=\"range\" id=\"sl-tol-bot\" min=\"0.1\" max=\"20\" step=\"0.1\" value=\"3\">\n    <span class=\"val\" id=\"val-tol-bot\">3.0px</span>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"status\" id=\"point-count\"></div>\n  <div class=\"info\">ドラッグで制御点を移動。ダブルクリックで制御点を追加。右クリックで制御点を削除。</div>\n</div>\n\n<canvas id=\"cv\" width=\"800\" height=\"400\"></canvas>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>誤差情報</h2>\n  <div id=\"error-info\" style=\"font-size:12px; white-space:pre; line-height:1.6;\"></div>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>エクスポート</h2>\n  <button class=\"primary\" onclick=\"exportPath()\">cat-path.json 用データをエクスポート</button>\n  <button onclick=\"navigator.clipboard.writeText(document.getElementById('export-data').value)\">クリップボードにコピー</button>\n  <textarea id=\"export-data\" readonly></textarea>\n</div>\n\n<script>\nconst W = 800, H = 400;\nconst canvas = document.getElementById('cv');\nconst ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n\nconst headImg = new Image();\nconst tailImg = new Image();\nlet imagesLoaded = false;\n\n// 抽出された輪郭 (生データ)\nlet extractedTop = [];\nlet extractedBottom = [];\n\n// 間引き後の制御点 (編集可能)\nlet ctrlTop = [];\nlet ctrlBottom = [];\n\n// ドラッグ状態\nlet dragging = null; // { line: 'top'|'bottom', index: number }\nconst DRAG_RADIUS = 8;\n\n// ============================================================\n// 画像読み込み・輪郭抽出\n// ============================================================\nfunction loadImages() {\n  return new Promise(resolve => {\n    let loaded = 0;\n    const onLoad = () => { if (++loaded === 2) { imagesLoaded = true; resolve(); } };\n    headImg.src = '../img/head.png';\n    tailImg.src = '../img/tail.png';\n    headImg.onload = onLoad;\n    tailImg.onload = onLoad;\n  });\n}\n\nfunction extractContours() {\n  const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');\n  offscreen.width = W;\n  offscreen.height = H;\n  const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');\n  octx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);\n  octx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);\n\n  const imageData = octx.getImageData(0, 0, W, H);\n  const pixels = imageData.data;\n  const threshold = 128;\n  const step = 2;\n\n  extractedTop = [];\n  extractedBottom = [];\n\n  for (let px = 0; px < W; px += step) {\n    let topOuter = -1, topInner = -1;\n    let bottomOuter = -1, bottomInner = -1;\n\n    for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {\n        topOuter = y;\n        for (let y2 = y + 1; y2 < H; y2++) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) { topInner = y2 - 1; break; }\n        }\n        if (topInner === -1) topInner = topOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (let y = H - 1; y >= 0; y--) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {\n        bottomOuter = y;\n        for (let y2 = y - 1; y2 >= 0; y2--) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) { bottomInner = y2 + 1; break; }\n        }\n        if (bottomInner === -1) bottomInner = bottomOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (topOuter !== -1) {\n      extractedTop.push({ x: px / W, y: ((topOuter + topInner) / 2) / H });\n    }\n    if (bottomOuter !== -1) {\n      extractedBottom.push({ x: px / W, y: ((bottomOuter + bottomInner) / 2) / H });\n    }\n  }\n\n  smoothPoints(extractedTop, 3);\n  smoothPoints(extractedBottom, 3);\n}\n\nfunction smoothPoints(pts, radius) {\n  const orig = pts.map(p => p.y);\n  for (let i = radius; i < pts.length - radius; i++) {\n    let sum = 0;\n    for (let j = -radius; j <= radius; j++) sum += orig[i + j];\n    pts[i].y = sum / (radius * 2 + 1);\n  }\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// Douglas-Peucker 間引き\n// ============================================================\nfunction douglasPeucker(points, tolerance) {\n  if (points.length <= 2) return points.map(p => ({ ...p }));\n\n  // toleranceはピクセル単位。座標はratio単位なのでY方向を変換\n  const tolY = tolerance / H;\n\n  let maxDist = 0;\n  let maxIdx = 0;\n  const first = points[0];\n  const last = points[points.length - 1];\n\n  for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    const d = perpendicularDist(points[i], first, last);\n    if (d > maxDist) {\n      maxDist = d;\n      maxIdx = i;\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (maxDist > tolY) {\n    const left = douglasPeucker(points.slice(0, maxIdx + 1), tolerance);\n    const right = douglasPeucker(points.slice(maxIdx), tolerance);\n    return left.slice(0, -1).concat(right);\n  } else {\n    return [{ ...first }, { ...last }];\n  }\n}\n\nfunction perpendicularDist(point, lineStart, lineEnd) {\n  const dx = lineEnd.x - lineStart.x;\n  const dy = lineEnd.y - lineStart.y;\n  const lenSq = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n  if (lenSq === 0) return Math.hypot(point.x - lineStart.x, point.y - lineStart.y);\n\n  const t = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, ((point.x - lineStart.x) * dx + (point.y - lineStart.y) * dy) / lenSq));\n  const projX = lineStart.x + t * dx;\n  const projY = lineStart.y + t * dy;\n  // Y方向の距離のみで判定（X方向は時系列的なので）\n  return Math.abs(point.y - projY);\n}\n\nfunction simplify() {\n  const tolTop = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sl-tol-top').value);\n  const tolBot = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sl-tol-bot').value);\n  document.getElementById('val-tol-top').textContent = tolTop.toFixed(1) + 'px';\n  document.getElementById('val-tol-bot').textContent = tolBot.toFixed(1) + 'px';\n\n  ctrlTop = douglasPeucker(extractedTop, tolTop);\n  ctrlBottom = douglasPeucker(extractedBottom, tolBot);\n\n  document.getElementById('point-count').textContent =\n    `上の線: ${ctrlTop.length}点 / 下の線: ${ctrlBottom.length}点`;\n\n  draw();\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// Catmull-Rom スプライン補間\n// ============================================================\nfunction catmullRomY(points, xRatio) {\n  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;\n  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;\n  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;\n\n  // xRatioが含まれるセグメントを探す\n  let seg = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }\n  }\n\n  const p0 = points[Math.max(0, seg - 1)];\n  const p1 = points[seg];\n  const p2 = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, seg + 1)];\n  const p3 = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, seg + 2)];\n\n  const segLen = p2.x - p1.x;\n  if (segLen === 0) return p1.y;\n  const t = (xRatio - p1.x) / segLen;\n\n  // Catmull-Rom (alpha=0.5, tension=0)\n  const t2 = t * t;\n  const t3 = t2 * t;\n  return 0.5 * (\n    (2 * p1.y) +\n    (-p0.y + p2.y) * t +\n    (2 * p0.y - 5 * p1.y + 4 * p2.y - p3.y) * t2 +\n    (-p0.y + 3 * p1.y - 3 * p2.y + p3.y) * t3\n  );\n}\n\nfunction drawSpline(points, color, width) {\n  if (points.length < 2) return;\n  ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n  ctx.lineWidth = width;\n  ctx.beginPath();\n\n  const startPx = Math.floor(points[0].x * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(points[points.length - 1].x * W);\n\n  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px++) {\n    const xr = px / W;\n    const y = catmullRomY(points, xr);\n    if (y === null) continue;\n    if (px === startPx) ctx.moveTo(px, y * H);\n    else ctx.lineTo(px, y * H);\n  }\n  ctx.stroke();\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// 描画\n// ============================================================\nfunction draw() {\n  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);\n\n  const showImage = document.getElementById('chk-image').checked;\n  const showContour = document.getElementById('chk-contour').checked;\n  const showSpline = document.getElementById('chk-spline').checked;\n  const showPoints = document.getElementById('chk-points').checked;\n  const showGrid = document.getElementById('chk-grid').checked;\n\n  // グリッド\n  if (showGrid) {\n    ctx.strokeStyle = '#eee';\n    ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 40) {\n      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, 0); ctx.lineTo(x, H); ctx.stroke();\n    }\n    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) {\n      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, y); ctx.lineTo(W, y); ctx.stroke();\n    }\n    ctx.fillStyle = '#aaa';\n    ctx.font = '9px monospace';\n    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 80) {\n      ctx.fillText((x / W).toFixed(2), x + 2, 10);\n    }\n    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) {\n      ctx.fillText((y / H).toFixed(2), 2, y + 10);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 元画像\n  if (showImage && imagesLoaded) {\n    ctx.save();\n    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.25;\n    ctx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);\n    ctx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);\n    ctx.restore();\n  }\n\n  // 抽出輪郭\n  if (showContour) {\n    drawPolyline(extractedTop, '#ff0000', 1);\n    drawPolyline(extractedBottom, '#0000ff', 1);\n  }\n\n  // スプライン曲線\n  if (showSpline) {\n    drawSpline(ctrlTop, '#00cc00', 2.5);\n    drawSpline(ctrlBottom, '#ff8800', 2.5);\n  }\n\n  // 制御点\n  if (showPoints) {\n    drawControlPoints(ctrlTop, '#00cc00', '#009900');\n    drawControlPoints(ctrlBottom, '#ff8800', '#cc6600');\n  }\n\n  // 誤差\n  computeErrors();\n}\n\nfunction drawPolyline(points, color, width) {\n  if (points.length < 2) return;\n  ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n  ctx.lineWidth = width;\n  ctx.beginPath();\n  ctx.moveTo(points[0].x * W, points[0].y * H);\n  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) {\n    ctx.lineTo(points[i].x * W, points[i].y * H);\n  }\n  ctx.stroke();\n}\n\nfunction drawControlPoints(points, fillColor, strokeColor) {\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n    const px = points[i].x * W;\n    const py = points[i].y * H;\n\n    ctx.fillStyle = fillColor;\n    ctx.strokeStyle = strokeColor;\n    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n    ctx.beginPath();\n    ctx.arc(px, py, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n    ctx.fill();\n    ctx.stroke();\n  }\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// 誤差計算\n// ============================================================\nfunction computeErrors() {\n  if (!ctrlTop.length || !ctrlBottom.length) return;\n\n  const lines = [];\n  let topErr = 0, topCount = 0;\n  let botErr = 0, botCount = 0;\n\n  for (const pt of extractedTop) {\n    const spY = catmullRomY(ctrlTop, pt.x);\n    if (spY !== null) {\n      const diff = (pt.y - spY) * H;\n      topErr += diff * diff;\n      topCount++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  for (const pt of extractedBottom) {\n    const spY = catmullRomY(ctrlBottom, pt.x);\n    if (spY !== null) {\n      const diff = (pt.y - spY) * H;\n      botErr += diff * diff;\n      botCount++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  const topRmse = topCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(topErr / topCount) : 0;\n  const botRmse = botCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(botErr / botCount) : 0;\n  const totalRmse = Math.sqrt((topErr + botErr) / (topCount + botCount));\n\n  lines.push(`上の線: RMSE ${topRmse.toFixed(2)}px (${ctrlTop.length}点, ${topCount}サンプル)`);\n  lines.push(`下の線: RMSE ${botRmse.toFixed(2)}px (${ctrlBottom.length}点, ${botCount}サンプル)`);\n  lines.push(`合計:   RMSE ${totalRmse.toFixed(2)}px`);\n\n  document.getElementById('error-info').innerHTML = lines.join('\\n');\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// ドラッグ操作\n// ============================================================\nfunction getMousePos(e) {\n  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n  return {\n    x: (e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width * W,\n    y: (e.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height * H\n  };\n}\n\nfunction findNearestPoint(mx, my) {\n  let best = null;\n  let bestDist = DRAG_RADIUS * DRAG_RADIUS;\n\n  for (let i = 0; i < ctrlTop.length; i++) {\n    const dx = ctrlTop[i].x * W - mx;\n    const dy = ctrlTop[i].y * H - my;\n    const d = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n    if (d < bestDist) { bestDist = d; best = { line: 'top', index: i }; }\n  }\n  for (let i = 0; i < ctrlBottom.length; i++) {\n    const dx = ctrlBottom[i].x * W - mx;\n    const dy = ctrlBottom[i].y * H - my;\n    const d = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n    if (d < bestDist) { bestDist = d; best = { line: 'bottom', index: i }; }\n  }\n  return best;\n}\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {\n  if (e.button !== 0) return;\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n  dragging = findNearestPoint(x, y);\n  if (dragging) {\n    canvas.style.cursor = 'grabbing';\n    e.preventDefault();\n  }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n\n  if (dragging) {\n    const pts = dragging.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n    const idx = dragging.index;\n    // X方向: 前後の点の間に制限（端点はX固定）\n    if (idx === 0 || idx === pts.length - 1) {\n      pts[idx].y = y / H;\n    } else {\n      const minX = pts[idx - 1].x + 0.001;\n      const maxX = pts[idx + 1].x - 0.001;\n      pts[idx].x = Math.max(minX, Math.min(maxX, x / W));\n      pts[idx].y = y / H;\n    }\n    draw();\n  } else {\n    const near = findNearestPoint(x, y);\n    canvas.style.cursor = near ? 'grab' : 'crosshair';\n  }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {\n  if (dragging) {\n    dragging = null;\n    canvas.style.cursor = 'crosshair';\n  }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {\n  if (dragging) {\n    dragging = null;\n    canvas.style.cursor = 'crosshair';\n  }\n});\n\n// ダブルクリック: 制御点を追加\ncanvas.addEventListener('dblclick', (e) => {\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n  const xr = x / W;\n  const yr = y / H;\n\n  // 上と下のスプラインのどちらに近いか判定\n  const topY = catmullRomY(ctrlTop, xr);\n  const botY = catmullRomY(ctrlBottom, xr);\n  const distTop = topY !== null ? Math.abs(yr - topY) : Infinity;\n  const distBot = botY !== null ? Math.abs(yr - botY) : Infinity;\n\n  const targetLine = distTop <= distBot ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n\n  // 挿入位置を探す\n  let insertIdx = targetLine.length;\n  for (let i = 0; i < targetLine.length; i++) {\n    if (targetLine[i].x > xr) { insertIdx = i; break; }\n  }\n\n  targetLine.splice(insertIdx, 0, { x: xr, y: yr });\n  draw();\n});\n\n// 右クリック: 制御点を削除\ncanvas.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {\n  e.preventDefault();\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n  const near = findNearestPoint(x, y);\n  if (near) {\n    const pts = near.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n    // 端点は削除しない\n    if (near.index > 0 && near.index < pts.length - 1) {\n      pts.splice(near.index, 1);\n      draw();\n    }\n  }\n});\n\n// ============================================================\n// エクスポート\n// ============================================================\nfunction exportPath() {\n  const round4 = v => Math.round(v * 10000) / 10000;\n  const data = {\n    comment: \"正解のねこの静的パス定義。制御点をCatmull-Romスプラインで補間。座標はキャンバス比率(0-1)。\",\n    topLine: ctrlTop.map(p => ({ x: round4(p.x), y: round4(p.y) })),\n    bottomLine: ctrlBottom.map(p => ({ x: round4(p.x), y: round4(p.y) }))\n  };\n  document.getElementById('export-data').value = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// スライダーイベント\n// ============================================================\ndocument.getElementById('sl-tol-top').addEventListener('input', simplify);\ndocument.getElementById('sl-tol-bot').addEventListener('input', simplify);\n\ndocument.querySelectorAll('input[type=checkbox]').forEach(el => {\n  el.addEventListener('change', draw);\n});\n\n// ============================================================\n// 初期化\n// ============================================================\nasync function init() {\n  await loadImages();\n  extractContours();\n  simplify();\n}\n\ninit();\n</script>\n</body>\n</html>\n"
}
```

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:05:09.207Z)*

*📤 結果:*

The file c:\dev\nekoegaku\tools\verify-path.html has been updated successfully.

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:05:17.972Z)*

パスエディタを構築しました。`tools/verify-path.html` をリロードしてください。

**使い方：**
- **許容誤差スライダー**: 左に動かすと点が増え精度UP、右に動かすと点が減り簡素に
- **ドラッグ**: 制御点をつかんで移動
- **ダブルクリック**: 近い線に制御点を追加
- **右クリック**: 制御点を削除（端点以外）
- **エクスポート**: 調整が終わったら「cat-path.json 用データをエクスポート」ボタンで出力

まずは許容誤差を調整して、上下それぞれ20-50点くらいの範囲で元画像にどの程度合うか確認してみてください。

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:09:26.614Z)*

仕組みはめっちゃいい感じなんですが、ベジェ曲線の制御点も動かせるようにすることってできますか？
点の位置は合ってるのに曲がり方が逆のやつがあって……

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:09:58.606Z)*

できます。各制御点に**接線ハンドル**を追加して、曲がり方を制御できるようにします。

Catmull-Romは自動で接線を計算しますが、それを上書きできる仕組み（Hermiteスプライン化）にします。

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:09:58.748Z)*

  "limit": 50
}
```

```
{
  "file_path": "c:\\dev\\nekoegaku\\tools\\verify-path.html",
  "content": "<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang=\"ja\">\n<head>\n<meta charset=\"UTF-8\">\n<title>ねこパスエディタ</title>\n<style>\n  * { box-sizing: border-box; }\n  body { margin: 20px; font-family: monospace; { font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: bold; margin: 5px 0; }\n</style>\n</head>\n<body>\n<h1>ねこパスエディタ</h1>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>表示</h2>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-image\" checked> 元画像</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-contour\" checked> 抽出輪郭</label>\n  <label><input type=\"checkbox\" id=\"chk-spline\" checked> スプライン曲線</label>\n グリッド</label>\n\n  <div class=\"legend\">\n    <span style=\"background:#ff0000\"></span>抽出輪郭(上)\n    <span style=\"background:#0000ff\"></span>抽出輪郭(下)\n    <span style=\"background:#00cc00\"></span>スプライン(上)\n    <span style=\"background:#ff8800\"></span>スプライン(下)\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>間引き (Douglas-Peucker)</h2>\n  <div class=\"slider-row\">\n    <label>上の線 許容誤差:</label>\n    <input type=\"range\" id=\"sl-tol-top\" min=\"0.1\" max=\"20\" step=\"0.1\" value=\"3\">\n    <span class=\"val\" id=\"val-tol-top\">3.0px</span>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"slider-row\">\n    <label>下の線 許容誤差:</label>\n    <input type=\"range\" id=\"sl-tol-bot\" min=\"0.1\" max=\"20\" step=\"0.1\" value=\"3\">\n    <span class=\"val\" id=\"val-tol-bot\">3.0px</span>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"status\" id=\"point-count\"></div>\n  <div class=\"info\">\n    ドラッグ: 制御点を移動 / ダブルクリック: 制御点を追加 / 右クリック: 制御点を削除<br>\n    Shift+ドラッグ: 接線ハンドルを表示して曲がり方を調整 / Shift+右クリック: 接線をリセット\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n<canvas id=\"cv\" width=\"800\" height=\"400\"></canvas>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>誤差情報</h2>\n  <div id=\"error-info\" style=\"font-size:12px; white-space:pre; line-height:1.6;\"></div>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"panel\">\n  <h2>エクスポート</h2>\n  <button class=\"primary\" onclick=\"exportPath()\">cat-path.json 用データをエクスポート</button>\n  <button onclick=\"navigator.clipboard.writeText(document.getElementById('export-data').value)\">クリップボードにコピー</button>\n  <textarea id=\"export-data\" readonly></textarea>\n</div>\n\n<script>\nconst W = 800, H = 400;\nconst canvas = document.getElementById('cv');\nconst ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n\nconst headImg = new Image();\nconst tailImg = new Image();\nlet imagesLoaded = false;\n\n// 抽出された輪郭 (生データ)\nlet extractedTop = [];\nlet extractedBottom = [];\n\n// 間引き後の制御点 (編集可能)\n// 各点: { x, y, tx?, ty? }\n//   tx, ty = カスタム接線ベクトル (未設定なら Catmull-Rom 自動計算)\nlet ctrlTop = [];\nlet ctrlBottom = [];\n\n// ドラッグ状態\nlet dragging = null;\n// { type: 'point'|'handle', line: 'top'|'bottom', index: number }\nconst DRAG_RADIUS = 8;\nconst HANDLE_RADIUS = 6;\nconst HANDLE_LEN = 40; // 接線ハンドルの表示長さ(px)\n\n// ============================================================\n// 画像読み込み・輪郭抽出\n// ============================================================\nfunction loadImages() {\n  return new Promise(resolve => {\n    let loaded = 0;\n    const onLoad = () => { if (++loaded === 2) { imagesLoaded = true; resolve(); } };\n    headImg.src = '../img/head.png';\n    tailImg.src = '../img/tail.png';\n    headImg.onload = onLoad;\n    tailImg.onload = onLoad;\n  });\n}\n\nfunction extractContours() {\n  const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');\n  offscreen.width = W;\n  offscreen.height = H;\n  const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');\n  octx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);\n  octx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);\n\n  const imageData = octx.getImageData(0, 0, W, H);\n  const pixels = imageData.data;\n  const threshold = 128;\n  const step = 2;\n\n  extractedTop = [];\n  extractedBottom = [];\n\n  for (let px = 0; px < W; px += step) {\n    let topOuter = -1, topInner = -1;\n    let bottomOuter = -1, bottomInner = -1;\n\n    for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {\n        topOuter = y;\n        for (let y2 = y + 1; y2 < H; y2++) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) { topInner = y2 - 1; break; }\n        }\n        if (topInner === -1) topInner = topOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (let y = H - 1; y >= 0; y--) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > threshold) {\n        bottomOuter = y;\n        for (let y2 = y - 1; y2 >= 0; y2--) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= threshold) { bottomInner = y2 + 1; break; }\n        }\n        if (bottomInner === -1) bottomInner = bottomOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (topOuter !== -1)\n      extractedTop.push({ x: px / W, y: ((topOuter + topInner) / 2) / H });\n    if (bottomOuter !== -1)\n      extractedBottom.push({ x: px / W, y: ((bottomOuter + bottomInner) / 2) / H });\n  }\n\n  smoothPoints(extractedTop, 3);\n  smoothPoints(extractedBottom, 3);\n}\n\nfunction smoothPoints(pts, radius) {\n  const orig = pts.map(p => p.y);\n  for (let i = radius; i < pts.length - radius; i++) {\n    let sum = 0;\n    for (let j = -radius; j <= radius; j++) sum += orig[i + j];\n    pts[i].y = sum / (radius * 2 + 1);\n  }\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// Douglas-Peucker 間引き\n// ============================================================\nfunction douglasPeucker(points, tolerance) {\n  if (points.length <= 2) return points.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y }));\n  const tolY = tolerance / H;\n\n  let maxDist = 0, maxIdx = 0;\n  const first = points[0], last = points[points.length - 1];\n\n  for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    const d = perpDist(points[i], first, last);\n    if (d > maxDist) { maxDist = d; maxIdx = i; }\n  }\n\n  if (maxDist > tolY) {\n    const left = douglasPeucker(points.slice(0, maxIdx + 1), tolerance);\n    const right = douglasPeucker(points.slice(maxIdx), tolerance);\n    return left.slice(0, -1).concat(right);\n  }\n  return [{ x: first.x, y: first.y }, { x: last.x, y: last.y }];\n}\n\nfunction perpDist(point, a, b) {\n  const dx = b.x - a.x, dy = b.y - a.y;\n  const lenSq = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n  if (lenSq === 0) return Math.abs(point.y - a.y);\n  const t = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, ((point.x - a.x) * dx + (point.y - a.y) * dy) / lenSq));\n  return Math.abs(point.y - (a.y + t * dy));\n}\n\nfunction simplify() {\n  const tolTop = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sl-tol-top').value);\n  const tolBot = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sl-tol-bot').value);\n  document.getElementById('val-tol-top').textContent = tolTop.toFixed(1) + 'px';\n  document.getElementById('val-tol-bot').textContent = tolBot.toFixed(1) + 'px';\n\n  ctrlTop = douglasPeucker(extractedTop, tolTop);\n  ctrlBottom = douglasPeucker(extractedBottom, tolBot);\n\n  document.getElementById('point-count').textContent =\n    `上の線: ${ctrlTop.length}点 / 下の線: ${ctrlBottom.length}点`;\n  draw();\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// Hermite スプライン補間 (Catmull-Rom + カスタム接線)\n// ============================================================\n\n// 点iの接線を取得。カスタム接線があればそれを使用、なければCatmull-Rom自動計算\nfunction getTangent(points, i) {\n  const p = points[i];\n  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) {\n    return { x: p.tx, y: p.ty };\n  }\n  // Catmull-Rom 自動接線: (p[i+1] - p[i-1]) / 2\n  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];\n  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];\n  return {\n    x: (next.x - prev.x) / 2,\n    y: (next.y - prev.y) / 2\n  };\n}\n\n// Hermite 補間で xRatio に対応する Y を返す\nfunction hermiteY(points, xRatio) {\n  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;\n  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;\n  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;\n\n  // セグメントを探す\n  let seg = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }\n  }\n\n  const p0 = points[seg];\n  const p1 = points[seg + 1];\n  const m0 = getTangent(points, seg);\n  const m1 = getTangent(points, seg + 1);\n\n  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;\n  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;\n  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;\n  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;\n\n  // Hermite 基底関数\n  const h00 = 2 * t3 - 3 * t2 + 1;\n  const h10 = t3 - 2 * t2 + t;\n  const h01 = -2 * t3 + 3 * t2;\n  const h11 = t3 - t2;\n\n  // 接線はセグメント長でスケール\n  return h00 * p0.y + h10 * m0.y * segLen / ((m0.x === 0 ? 1 : m0.x)) * segLen\n    // ... 複雑になるので、元のCatmull-Romの定式化に近い形で実装\n    ? hermiteSimple(p0, p1, m0, m1, t)\n    : p0.y;\n}\n\n// シンプルなHermite補間 (Catmull-Rom互換)\nfunction hermiteSimple(p0, p1, m0, m1, t) {\n  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;\n  // Catmull-Rom式: y成分のみ補間、接線のy成分を使用\n  return (2 * t3 - 3 * t2 + 1) * p0.y\n       + (t3 - 2 * t2 + t) * m0.y\n       + (-2 * t3 + 3 * t2) * p1.y\n       + (t3 - t2) * m1.y;\n}\n\n// 実際の補間関数\nfunction splineY(points, xRatio) {\n  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;\n  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;\n  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;\n\n  let seg = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }\n  }\n\n  const p0 = points[seg];\n  const p1 = points[seg + 1];\n\n  const segLenX = p1.x - p0.x;\n  if (segLenX === 0) return p0.y;\n  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLenX;\n\n  // 各点の接線(y成分)を取得\n  // Catmull-Rom: m_i = (p_{i+1}.y - p_{i-1}.y) / 2  ただしtはセグメント間で正規化\n  // カスタム接線がある場合はそれを使う\n  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);\n  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);\n\n  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;\n  return (2 * t3 - 3 * t2 + 1) * p0.y\n       + (t3 - 2 * t2 + t) * tanY0\n       + (-2 * t3 + 3 * t2) * p1.y\n       + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;\n}\n\n// Hermite用のスケール済み接線Y成分\nfunction getScaledTanY(points, i) {\n  const p = points[i];\n  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) {\n    // カスタム接線: ty はそのまま使う (すでにスケール済み想定)\n    return p.ty;\n  }\n  // Catmull-Rom デフォルト接線\n  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];\n  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];\n  return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// 接線ハンドルの表示位置を計算\n// ============================================================\nfunction getHandlePos(points, i) {\n  const p = points[i];\n  const tanY = getScaledTanY(points, i);\n\n  // 接線の方向を計算 (Catmull-Romの場合)\n  let tanX;\n  if (p.tx !== undefined) {\n    tanX = p.tx;\n  } else {\n    const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];\n    const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];\n    tanX = (next.x - prev.x) / 2;\n  }\n\n  // 正規化してハンドル長さに\n  const len = Math.sqrt((tanX * W) ** 2 + (tanY * H) ** 2);\n  if (len === 0) return { x: p.x * W + HANDLE_LEN, y: p.y * H };\n\n  const scale = HANDLE_LEN / len;\n  return {\n    // ハンドルは接線の正方向\n    x: p.x * W + tanX * W * scale,\n    y: p.y * H + tanY * H * scale\n  };\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// 描画\n// ============================================================\nfunction drawSpline(points, color, width) {\n  if (points.length < 2) return;\n  ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n  ctx.lineWidth = width;\n  ctx.beginPath();\n\n  const startPx = Math.floor(points[0].x * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(points[points.length - 1].x * W);\n\n  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px++) {\n    const xr = px / W;\n    const y = splineY(points, xr);\n    if (y === null) continue;\n    if (px === startPx) ctx.moveTo(px, y * H);\n    else ctx.lineTo(px, y * H);\n  }\n  ctx.stroke();\n}\n\nfunction draw() {\n  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);\n\n  const showImage = document.getElementById('chk-image').checked;\n  const showContour = document.getElementById('chk-contour').checked;\n  const showSpline = document.getElementById('chk-spline').checked;\n  const showPoints = document.getElementById('chk-points').checked;\n  const showHandles = document.getElementById('chk-handles').checked;\n  const showGrid = document.getElementById('chk-grid').checked;\n\n  if (showGrid) {\n    ctx.strokeStyle = '#eee';\n    ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 40) {\n      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, 0); ctx.lineTo(x, H); ctx.stroke();\n    }\n    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) {\n      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, y); ctx.lineTo(W, y); ctx.stroke();\n    }\n    ctx.fillStyle = '#aaa';\n    ctx.font = '9px monospace';\n    for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 80) ctx.fillText((x / W).toFixed(2), x + 2, 10);\n    for (let y = 0; y <= H; y += 40) ctx.fillText((y / H).toFixed(2), 2, y + 10);\n  }\n\n  if (showImage && imagesLoaded) {\n    ctx.save();\n    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.25;\n    ctx.drawImage(headImg, 0, 0, W / 2, H);\n    ctx.drawImage(tailImg, W / 2, 0, W / 2, H);\n    ctx.restore();\n  }\n\n  if (showContour) {\n    drawPolyline(extractedTop, '#ff0000', 1);\n    drawPolyline(extractedBottom, '#0000ff', 1);\n  }\n\n  if (showSpline) {\n    drawSpline(ctrlTop, '#00cc00', 2.5);\n    drawSpline(ctrlBottom, '#ff8800', 2.5);\n  }\n\n  if (showPoints || showHandles) {\n    drawCtrlPoints(ctrlTop, '#00cc00', '#009900', showPoints, showHandles);\n    drawCtrlPoints(ctrlBottom, '#ff8800', '#cc6600', showPoints, showHandles);\n  }\n\n  computeErrors();\n}\n\nfunction drawPolyline(points, color, width) {\n  if (points.length < 2) return;\n  ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n  ctx.lineWidth = width;\n  ctx.beginPath();\n  ctx.moveTo(points[0].x * W, points[0].y * H);\n  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) ctx.lineTo(points[i].x * W, points[i].y * H);\n  ctx.stroke();\n}\n\nfunction drawCtrlPoints(points, fill, stroke, showPts, showHandles) {\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n    const px = points[i].x * W;\n    const py = points[i].y * H;\n\n    if (showHandles || points[i].tx !== undefined) {\n      // 接線ハンドルを描画\n      const hp = getHandlePos(points, i);\n      const hasCustom = points[i].tx !== undefined;\n\n      // ハンドル線\n      ctx.strokeStyle = hasCustom ? '#e74c3c' : 'rgba(150,150,150,0.5)';\n      ctx.lineWidth = hasCustom ? 1.5 : 1;\n      ctx.setLineDash([3, 3]);\n      ctx.beginPath();\n      // 逆方向にも描画\n      ctx.moveTo(2 * px - hp.x, 2 * py - hp.y);\n      ctx.lineTo(hp.x, hp.y);\n      ctx.stroke();\n      ctx.setLineDash([]);\n\n      // ハンドル点\n      ctx.fillStyle = hasCustom ? '#e74c3c' : 'rgba(150,150,150,0.6)';\n      ctx.strokeStyle = hasCustom ? '#c0392b' : '#999';\n      ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n      ctx.beginPath();\n      ctx.arc(hp.x, hp.y, HANDLE_RADIUS - 1, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n      ctx.fill();\n      ctx.stroke();\n\n      // 逆側のハンドル点\n      ctx.beginPath();\n      ctx.arc(2 * px - hp.x, 2 * py - hp.y, HANDLE_RADIUS - 1, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n      ctx.fill();\n      ctx.stroke();\n    }\n\n    if (showPts) {\n      // 制御点本体\n      ctx.fillStyle = fill;\n      ctx.strokeStyle = stroke;\n      ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n      ctx.beginPath();\n      ctx.arc(px, py, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n      ctx.fill();\n      ctx.stroke();\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// 誤差計算\n// ============================================================\nfunction computeErrors() {\n  if (!ctrlTop.length || !ctrlBottom.length) return;\n\n  let topErr = 0, topCount = 0;\n  let botErr = 0, botCount = 0;\n\n  for (const pt of extractedTop) {\n    const sy = splineY(ctrlTop, pt.x);\n    if (sy !== null) { const d = (pt.y - sy) * H; topErr += d * d; topCount++; }\n  }\n  for (const pt of extractedBottom) {\n    const sy = splineY(ctrlBottom, pt.x);\n    if (sy !== null) { const d = (pt.y - sy) * H; botErr += d * d; botCount++; }\n  }\n\n  const topRmse = topCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(topErr / topCount) : 0;\n  const botRmse = botCount > 0 ? Math.sqrt(botErr / botCount) : 0;\n  const totalRmse = Math.sqrt((topErr + botErr) / (topCount + botCount));\n\n  const customTopCount = ctrlTop.filter(p => p.tx !== undefined).length;\n  const customBotCount = ctrlBottom.filter(p => p.tx !== undefined).length;\n\n  document.getElementById('error-info').innerHTML =\n    `上の線: RMSE ${topRmse.toFixed(2)}px (${ctrlTop.length}点, 接線カスタム${customTopCount}点)\\n` +\n    `下の線: RMSE ${botRmse.toFixed(2)}px (${ctrlBottom.length}点, 接線カスタム${customBotCount}点)\\n` +\n    `合計:   RMSE ${totalRmse.toFixed(2)}px`;\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// マウス操作\n// ============================================================\nfunction getMousePos(e) {\n  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n  return { x: (e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width * W, y: (e.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height * H };\n}\n\nfunction findNearest(mx, my, shiftKey) {\n  let best = null;\n  let bestDist = Infinity;\n\n  const search = (points, lineName) => {\n    for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n      // 接線ハンドル (Shiftキー押下時 or 常時)\n      if (shiftKey || points[i].tx !== undefined) {\n        const hp = getHandlePos(points, i);\n        let d = (hp.x - mx) ** 2 + (hp.y - my) ** 2;\n        if (d < bestDist && d < (HANDLE_RADIUS + 4) ** 2) {\n          bestDist = d; best = { type: 'handle', line: lineName, index: i, side: 1 };\n        }\n        // 逆側\n        const rhx = 2 * points[i].x * W - hp.x;\n        const rhy = 2 * points[i].y * H - hp.y;\n        d = (rhx - mx) ** 2 + (rhy - my) ** 2;\n        if (d < bestDist && d < (HANDLE_RADIUS + 4) ** 2) {\n          bestDist = d; best = { type: 'handle', line: lineName, index: i, side: -1 };\n        }\n      }\n\n      // 制御点本体\n      const dx = points[i].x * W - mx, dy = points[i].y * H - my;\n      const d = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n      if (d < bestDist && d < (DRAG_RADIUS + 2) ** 2) {\n        bestDist = d; best = { type: 'point', line: lineName, index: i };\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  search(ctrlTop, 'top');\n  search(ctrlBottom, 'bottom');\n  return best;\n}\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {\n  if (e.button !== 0) return;\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n  dragging = findNearest(x, y, e.shiftKey);\n\n  // Shift+クリックで制御点近くをクリック → ハンドルを出す\n  if (!dragging && e.shiftKey) {\n    const nearPt = findNearest(x, y, false);\n    if (nearPt && nearPt.type === 'point') {\n      // この点のハンドルを表示開始 (カスタム接線をセット)\n      const pts = nearPt.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n      const p = pts[nearPt.index];\n      if (p.tx === undefined) {\n        // 現在の自動接線を初期値としてセット\n        const prev = pts[Math.max(0, nearPt.index - 1)];\n        const next = pts[Math.min(pts.length - 1, nearPt.index + 1)];\n        p.tx = (next.x - prev.x) / 2;\n        p.ty = (next.y - prev.y) / 2;\n      }\n      dragging = { type: 'handle', line: nearPt.line, index: nearPt.index, side: 1 };\n      document.getElementById('chk-handles').checked = true;\n      draw();\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (dragging) {\n    canvas.style.cursor = 'grabbing';\n    e.preventDefault();\n  }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n\n  if (dragging) {\n    const pts = dragging.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n    const idx = dragging.index;\n\n    if (dragging.type === 'point') {\n      if (idx === 0 || idx === pts.length - 1) {\n        pts[idx].y = y / H;\n      } else {\n        const minX = pts[idx - 1].x + 0.001;\n        const maxX = pts[idx + 1].x - 0.001;\n        pts[idx].x = Math.max(minX, Math.min(maxX, x / W));\n        pts[idx].y = y / H;\n      }\n    } else if (dragging.type === 'handle') {\n      const p = pts[idx];\n      // ハンドル位置からベクトルを逆算\n      let hx, hy;\n      if (dragging.side === 1) {\n        hx = x / W - p.x;\n        hy = y / H - p.y;\n      } else {\n        // 逆側ハンドル: 反転\n        hx = p.x - x / W;\n        hy = p.y - y / H;\n      }\n\n      // ハンドル表示長さからスケール逆算してtx,tyに戻す\n      const displayLen = Math.sqrt((hx * W) ** 2 + (hy * H) ** 2);\n      if (displayLen > 0) {\n        // 接線の大きさは、自動計算時と同等のスケールに正規化\n        const prev = pts[Math.max(0, idx - 1)];\n        const next = pts[Math.min(pts.length - 1, idx + 1)];\n        const autoTx = (next.x - prev.x) / 2;\n        const autoTy = (next.y - prev.y) / 2;\n        const autoLen = Math.sqrt((autoTx * W) ** 2 + (autoTy * H) ** 2);\n        const scale = autoLen / displayLen;\n\n        p.tx = hx * scale;\n        p.ty = hy * scale;\n      }\n    }\n    draw();\n  } else {\n    const near = findNearest(x, y, e.shiftKey);\n    canvas.style.cursor = near ? 'grab' : 'crosshair';\n  }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {\n  if (dragging) { dragging = null; canvas.style.cursor = 'crosshair'; }\n});\n\ncanvas.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {\n  if (dragging) { dragging = null; canvas.style.cursor = 'crosshair'; }\n});\n\n// ダブルクリック: 制御点を追加\ncanvas.addEventListener('dblclick', (e) => {\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n  const xr = x / W, yr = y / H;\n\n  const topY = splineY(ctrlTop, xr);\n  const botY = splineY(ctrlBottom, xr);\n  const distTop = topY !== null ? Math.abs(yr - topY) : Infinity;\n  const distBot = botY !== null ? Math.abs(yr - botY) : Infinity;\n  const targetLine = distTop <= distBot ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n\n  let insertIdx = targetLine.length;\n  for (let i = 0; i < targetLine.length; i++) {\n    if (targetLine[i].x > xr) { insertIdx = i; break; }\n  }\n  targetLine.splice(insertIdx, 0, { x: xr, y: yr });\n  draw();\n});\n\n// 右クリック\ncanvas.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {\n  e.preventDefault();\n  const { x, y } = getMousePos(e);\n\n  if (e.shiftKey) {\n    // Shift+右クリック: 接線をリセット\n    const near = findNearest(x, y, true);\n    if (near) {\n      const pts = near.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n      delete pts[near.index].tx;\n      delete pts[near.index].ty;\n      draw();\n    }\n  } else {\n    // 右クリック: 制御点を削除\n    const near = findNearest(x, y, false);\n    if (near && near.type === 'point') {\n      const pts = near.line === 'top' ? ctrlTop : ctrlBottom;\n      if (near.index > 0 && near.index < pts.length - 1) {\n        pts.splice(near.index, 1);\n        draw();\n      }\n    }\n  }\n});\n\n// ============================================================\n// エクスポート\n// ============================================================\nfunction exportPath() {\n  const round4 = v => Math.round(v * 10000) / 10000;\n  const mapPt = p => {\n    const out = { x: round4(p.x), y: round4(p.y) };\n    if (p.tx !== undefined) { out.tx = round4(p.tx); out.ty = round4(p.ty); }\n    return out;\n  };\n  const data = {\n    comment: \"正解のねこの静的パス定義。Hermiteスプライン(Catmull-Rom + カスタム接線)で補間。座標はキャンバス比率(0-1)。\",\n    topLine: ctrlTop.map(mapPt),\n    bottomLine: ctrlBottom.map(mapPt)\n  };\n  document.getElementById('export-data').value = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// イベント\n// ============================================================\ndocument.getElementById('sl-tol-top').addEventListener('input', simplify);\ndocument.getElementById('sl-tol-bot').addEventListener('input', simplify);\ndocument.querySelectorAll('input[type=checkbox]').forEach(el => el.addEventListener('change', draw));\n\n// ============================================================\n// 初期化\n// ============================================================\nasync function init() {\n  await loadImages();\n  extractContours();\n  simplify();\n}\n\ninit();\n</script>\n</body>\n</html>\n"
}
```

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:12:03.712Z)*

リロードしてください。接線ハンドルの操作方法：

- **Shift+ドラッグ**: 制御点の近くでShiftを押しながらドラッグすると接線ハンドル（赤い点と破線）が出現し、曲がり方を調整できます
- **接線ハンドルをドラッグ**: 一度出したハンドルは直接ドラッグして調整
- **Shift+右クリック**: カスタム接線をリセットして自動計算に戻す
- **「接線ハンドル」チェックボックス**: 全点の接線ハンドルを一括表示

カスタム接線が設定された点は赤いハンドルで表示されます（未設定はグレー）。曲がり方が逆の箇所でハンドルの向きを調整してみてください。

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:19:27.801Z)*

はい、前の点より左(後の点より右)に行けないガードです。スプライン補間がX座標の昇順を前提にしているので、順序が入れ替わると曲線が壊れます。

ただ、**移動後に自動ソート**すれば破綻しません。やってみます。

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:21:07.708Z)*

そうです、おっしゃる通りです。「Y = f(X)」の関数として扱うために上下分離しています。しっぽの先端のようにX方向に折り返す部分は本来1本のパスで描きたいところですが、軸回転アプローチは確かに複雑になるので、現方式で進めましょう。

パスの調整作業を進めてもらって、いい感じになったら「エクスポート」ボタンでJSONを出力してください。それを `cat-path.json` に反映して次のステップに進みます。

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:30:07.744Z)*

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user wants to completely overhaul the "nekoegaku" (cat drawing game) architecture. Currently, the game extracts contours from hand-drawn cat images (head.png + tail.png) at runtime using pixel scanning (LUT-based approach). The user wants to:
   - Pre-define the "correct cat" path as static data (no runtime image analysis)
   - Claude Code analyzes images and defines paths, user verifies visually and adjusts
   - Split the path into segments and fit mathematical functions for slider control
   - Keep the UI unchanged (sliders can change in type/number)
   - Slider design to be decided AFTER path data is confirmed
   - Game display continues showing hand-drawn images (not mathematical curves)
   - New code integrated into game.js (no separate files)

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Douglas-Peucker algorithm**: Line simplification to reduce ~375 contour points to ~20-50 manageable control points
   - **Catmull-Rom splines**: Initial interpolation approach (control points lie on curve)
   - **Hermite splines**: Final interpolation approach (Catmull-Rom + custom tangent overrides for curvature control)
   - **Custom tangent handles**: tx/ty values on control points override auto-computed Catmull-Rom tangents
   - **LUT (Lookup Table)**: Current system extracts contours from images, builds baseline LUTs, adds parametric contributions (ears=gaussian, tail=smoothstep, feet=sine wave)
   - **RMSE scoring**: Player's curve vs correct curve comparison
   - **Monotonic X constraint**: Upper and lower contour lines must be functions of X (no X-direction backtracking), which is why the cat outline is split into top and bottom lines

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **c:\dev\nekoegaku\js\game.js** (862 lines)
     - Main game logic, the primary target for modification

   - **c:\dev\nekoegaku\tools\verify-path.html**
     - Interactive path editor tool built during this conversation
     - Features: Douglas-Peucker simplification, Hermite spline rendering, drag-to-edit control points, tangent handle editing (Shift+drag), right-click delete, double-click add, JSON export
     - Hermite spline implementation (key functions to reuse in game.js):
     ```javascript
     function getScaledTanY(points, i) {
       const p = points[i];
       if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) return p.ty;
       const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];
       const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];
       return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;
     }

     function splineY(points, xRatio) {
       if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;
       if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;
       if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;
       let seg = 0;
       for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
         if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }
       }
       const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];
       const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;
       if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;
       const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;
       const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);
       const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);
       const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;
       return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0
            + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;
     }
     ```

   - **c:\dev\nekoegaku\config\settings.json**

     - Some sections (answerParams, strokeBounds, strokeJunctions) may move to cat-path.json or be removed later

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Initial cat-path.json was completely wrong**: My visual estimates for coordinates were way off from the actual image. Fixed by using the browser-based contour extraction tool to get real pixel data and replacing the file with extracted data.
   - **Key naming mismatch**: verify-path.html referenced `catPath.topBaseline`/`catPath.bottomBaseline` but cat-path.json used `topLine`/`bottomLine`. Fixed with find-and-replace.
   - **Removed checkbox but left JS reference**: Removed `chk-baseline` checkbox HTML but left `document.getElementById('chk-baseline').checked` in draw(), causing TypeError. Fixed by removing the JS reference line.
   - **Endpoint X-movement restriction**: Endpoints of top/bottom lines were restricted to Y-only movement (`if (idx === 0 || idx === pts.length - 1) pts[idx].y = y / H`). User reported this. Fixed by removing the special case and using general min/max bounds.
   - **User feedback on endpoint fix**: User said "動かせるようになってませんよ" (still can't move). Was a browser cache issue - code was correct after Ctrl+Shift+R.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **Image analysis limitations**: User noted that the extracted contour (red/blue lines) doesn't perfectly match the original image, especially at top/bottom junction points. This is a limitation of the pixel scanning approach and can't be fixed by Claude since it can't see the actual rendering. Solution: the path editor lets the user manually adjust control points to match what they see.
   - **Catmull-Rom curvature issues**: User reported "点の位置は合ってるのに曲がり方が逆のやつがある" (some curves bend the wrong way). Solved by upgrading from Catmull-Rom to Hermite splines with custom tangent handles (tx/ty overrides).
   - **Monotonic X constraint**: The spline system requires X-monotonic points (each point must have a larger X than the previous). This means the cat outline must be split into top/bottom lines and can't represent X-backtracking shapes (like the tail tip curving back). User accepted this limitation.

    12→async function loadLang() {

    22→  document.getElementById('title-subtitle').textContent = LANG.subtitle;

    73→  Object.assign(player, CFG.playerDefaults);
    74→}

    76→// ============================================================
    77→// 上の線のy座標を計算
    78→// ============================================================
    79→function getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H) {
    80→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
    81→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
    82→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return CAT.noseY * H;
    83→
    84→  // LUTベースライン（元画像から抽出した固定パス）
    85→  const baseline = interpolateBaseline(refTopBaseline, xRatio);
    86→  if (baseline !== null) {
    87→    const ears = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);
    88→    const tail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
    89→    return baseline - ears - tail;
    90→  }
    91→
    92→  // フォールバック: 数式ベースライン
    93→  const backY = CAT.backY * H;
    94→  const noseY = CAT.noseY * H;
    95→  const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);
    96→  const faceY = faceT * (noseY - backY);
    97→
    98→  const ears = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);
    99→  const tail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   100→
```

100→
   101→  return backY + faceY - ears - tail;

   104→// ============================================================
   105→// 下の線のy座標を計算
   106→// ============================================================
   107→function getBottomY(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   108→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   109→  const BL = CFG.bottomLine;
   110→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   111→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return CAT.noseY * H;
   112→
   113→  // LUTベースライン（元画像から抽出した固定パス）
   114→  const baseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xRatio);
   115→  if (baseline !== null) {
   116→    const feet = getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   117→    return baseline + feet;
   118→  }
   119→
   120→  // フォールバック: LUT未構築時は平坦なベースライン
   121→  const noseY = CAT.noseY * H;
   122→  const bottomBaseY = CAT.bottomY * H;
   123→
   124→  let baseY;
   125→  if (t < BL.faceEndT) {
   126→    baseY = noseY + (bottomBaseY - noseY) * (t / BL.faceEndT);
   127→  } else {
   128→    baseY = bottomBaseY;
   129→  }
   130→
   131→  const feet = getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   132→  return baseY + feet;
   133→}

   138→function drawCat(ctx, params, color, lineWidth, alpha) {
   139→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   140→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   141→  const SC = CFG.strokeColors;
   142→  const W = ctx.canvas.width;
   143→  const H = ctx.canvas.height;
   144→  ctx.save();
   145→  ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
   146→  ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
   147→  ctx.lineCap = 'round';
   148→  ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
   149→
   150→  const SJ = CFG.strokeJunctions;
   151→
   152→  // ストローク1: 顔（earZoneStartX → faceBottomEndX を3次ベジェ曲線1本で描画）
   153→  ctx.strokeStyle = SC.face;
   154→  ctx.beginPath();
   155→  {
   156→    const x0 = SB.earZoneStartX * W;
   157→    const y0 = SJ.earZoneStart_topY * H;
   158→    const x3 = SB.faceBottomEndX * W;
   159→    const y3 = SJ.faceBottomEnd_bottomY * H;
   160→    const cp1x = x0 - 52;
   161→    const cp1y = y0 + 40;
   162→    const cp2x = x3 - 110;
   163→    const cp2y = y3 - 10;
   164→    ctx.moveTo(x0, y0);
   165→    ctx.bezierCurveTo(cp1x, cp1y, cp2x, cp2y, x3, y3);
   166→  }
   167→  ctx.stroke();
   168→
   169→  // ストローク2: 耳（earZoneStartX～earZoneEndX の上の線を1ストロークで描画）
   170→  ctx.strokeStyle = SC.ears;
   171→  ctx.beginPath();
   172→  for (let px = Math.floor(SB.earZoneStartX * W); px <= Math.ceil(SB.earZoneEndX * W); px++) {
   173→    const xr = px / W;
   174→    let y;
   175→    if (px === Math.floor(SB.earZoneStartX * W))  y = SJ.earZoneStart_topY * H;
   176→    else if (px === Math.ceil(SB.earZoneEndX * W)) y = SJ.earZoneEnd_topY * H;
   177→    else                                            y = getTopY(xr, params, W, H);
   178→    if (px === Math.floor(SB.earZoneStartX * W)) ctx.moveTo(px, y);
   179→    else ctx.lineTo(px, y);
   180→  }
   181→  ctx.stroke();
   182→
   183→  // ストローク3: 背中
   184→  ctx.strokeStyle = SC.back;
   185→  ctx.beginPath();
   186→  {
   187→    const x0 = SB.earZoneEndX * W;
   188→    const y0 = SJ.earZoneEnd_topY * H;
   189→    const x1 = SB.tailTopStartX * W;
   190→    const y1 = SJ.tailTopStart_topY * H;
   191→    const cpx = (x0 + x1) / 2;
   192→    const cpy = Math.min(y0, y1) - 5;
   193→    ctx.moveTo(x0, y0);
   194→    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cpx, cpy, x1, y1);
   195→  }
   196→  ctx.stroke();
   197→
   198→  // ストローク4: しっぽ（上の線 → 先端 → 下の線）
   199→  ctx.strokeStyle = SC.tail;
```

300→  drawTargetImage(octx, 1.0);
   301→
   302→  const imageData = octx.getImageData(0, 0, W, H);
   303→  const pixels = imageData.data;
   304→
   305→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   306→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   307→  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;
   308→
   309→  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   310→  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   311→
   312→  let idx = 0;
   313→  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   314→    let topOuter = -1;
   315→    let topInner = -1;
   316→    let bottomOuter = -1;
   317→    let bottomInner = -1;
   318→
   319→    // 上の線：外端（上端）を見つけてから、線の内端（下端）を探す
   320→    for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {
   321→      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > SC.alphaThreshold) {
   322→        topOuter = y;
   323→        // 線の内端（最初の透明ピクセル）を探す
   324→        for (let y2 = y + 1; y2 < H; y2++) {
   325→          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= SC.alphaThreshold) {
   326→            topInner = y2 - 1;
   327→            break;
   328→          }
   329→        }
   330→        if (topInner === -1) topInner = topOuter;
   331→        break;
   332→      }
   333→    }
   334→
   335→    // 下の線：外端（下端）を見つけてから、線の内端（上端）を探す
   336→    for (let y = H - 1; y >= 0; y--) {
   337→      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > SC.alphaThreshold) {
   338→        bottomOuter = y;
   339→        // 線の内端（最初の透明ピクセル）を探す
   340→        const xr_bottom = px / W;
   341→        const nearFeetEnd = xr_bottom >= SB.feetEndX - 0.02;
   342→        const nearFeetStart = xr_bottom <= SB.feetStartX + 0.00;
   343→        const maxLineSearch = (nearFeetEnd || nearFeetStart)
   344→          ? CFG.drawing.playerLineWidth * 3 : H;
   345→        for (let y2 = y - 1; y2 >= Math.max(0, y - maxLineSearch); y2--) {
   346→          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= SC.alphaThreshold) {
   347→            bottomInner = y2 + 1;
   348→            break;
   349→          }
   350→        }
   351→        if (bottomInner === -1) bottomInner = bottomOuter;
   352→        break;
   353→      }
   354→    }
   355→
   356→    // 線の中央を基準にする
   357→    let topFound = topOuter !== -1 ? (topOuter + topInner) / 2 : -1;
   358→    let bottomFound = bottomOuter !== -1 ? (bottomOuter + bottomInner) / 2 : -1;
   359→
   360→    if (topFound === -1) topFound = idx > 0 ? refTopY[idx - 1] : CAT.backY * H;
   361→    if (bottomFound === -1) bottomFound = idx > 0 ? refBottomY[idx - 1] : CAT.bottomY * H;
   362→
   363→    refTopY[idx] = topFound;
   364→    refBottomY[idx] = bottomFound;
   365→    idx++;
   366→  }

   382→

   384→
   385→function smoothContour(arr, radius) {
   386→  const copy = new Float64Array(arr);
   387→  for (let i = radius; i < arr.length - radius; i++) {
   388→    let sum = 0;
   389→    for (let j = -radius; j <= radius; j++) sum += copy[i + j];
   390→    arr[i] = sum / (radius * 2 + 1);
   391→  }
   392→}

   397→function getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W) {
   398→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   399→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:30:17.488Z)*

```
400→  const ear1X = (CAT.earCenterX - params.earGap / W) * W;
   401→  const ear2X = (CAT.earCenterX + params.earGap / W) * W;
   402→  const x = xRatio * W;
   403→  const ear1 = params.earHeight * Math.exp(-((x - ear1X) ** 2) / (2 * params.earWidth ** 2));
   404→  const ear2 = params.earHeight * Math.exp(-((x - ear2X) ** 2) / (2 * params.earWidth ** 2));
   405→  const span = CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX;
   406→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / span;
   407→  const earStartT = (SB.earZoneStartX - CAT.noseX) / span;
   408→  const earEndT = (SB.earZoneEndX - CAT.noseX) / span;
   409→  const fadeWidth = CFG.bottomLine.fadeWidth;
   410→  const envLeft = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (t - earStartT) / fadeWidth));
   411→  const envRight = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (earEndT - t) / fadeWidth));
   412→  return (ear1 + ear2) * envLeft * envRight;
   413→}
   414→
   415→function getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   416→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   417→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   418→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return 0;
   419→  const tailStart = (CFG.strokeBounds.tailTopStartX - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   420→  const tailT = Math.max(0, (t - tailStart) / (1 - tailStart));
   421→  const smoothTail = tailT * tailT * (3 - 2 * tailT);
   422→  return params.tailHeight * smoothTail;
   423→}
   424→
   425→function getTopYNoEars(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   426→  return getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H) + getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);
   427→}
   428→
   429→function getSingleEarContribution(xRatio, earCenterPx, params, W) {
   430→  const x = xRatio * W;
   431→  return params.earHeight * Math.exp(-((x - earCenterPx) ** 2) / (2 * params.earWidth ** 2));
   432→}
   433→
   434→function getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   435→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   436→  const BL = CFG.bottomLine;
   437→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   438→  const span = CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX;
   439→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / span;
   440→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return 0;
   441→  const feetStartT = (SB.feetStartX - CAT.noseX) / span - BL.fadeWidth;
   442→  const feetEndT = (SB.feetEndX - CAT.noseX) / span + BL.fadeWidth;
   443→  const feetEnvLeft = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (t - feetStartT) / BL.fadeWidth));
   444→  const feetEnvRight = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (feetEndT - t) / BL.fadeWidth));
   445→  const feetEnv = feetEnvLeft * feetEnvRight;
   446→  const wave = params.feetAmp * Math.sin(params.feetFreq * Math.PI * 2 * t + params.feetPhase);
   447→  return feetEnv * wave;
   448→}
   449→
   450→function buildBaselineLUT() {
   451→  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) return;
   452→
   453→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   454→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   455→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   456→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   457→  const answer = CFG.answerParams;
   458→
   459→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   460→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   461→  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;
   462→
   463→  refTopBaseline = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   464→  refBottomBaseline = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   465→
   466→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   467→  const SJ = CFG.strokeJunctions;
   468→
   469→  let idx = 0;
   470→  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   471→    const xr = px / W;
   472→    // 上線: baseline = refTopY + ears + tail (可変部分を足し戻す)
   473→    refTopBaseline[idx] = refTopY[idx]
   474→      + getEarContribution(xr, answer, W)
   475→      + getTailContribution(xr, answer, W, H);
   476→    // 下線: baseline = refBottomY - feet (可変部分を引き戻す)
   477→    // 足の右端以降はrefBottomYがお尻/しっぽの線を拾うため、端点値で固定
   478→    let bottomBase;
   479→    if (xr >= SB.feetEndX) {
   480→      bottomBase = SJ.feetEnd_bottomY * H;
   481→    } else {
   482→      bottomBase = refBottomY[idx]
   483→        - getFeetContribution(xr, answer, W, H);
   484→    }
   485→    refBottomBaseline[idx] = bottomBase;
   486→    idx++;
   487→  }
   488→}
   489→
   490→function interpolateBaseline(lut, xRatio) {
   491→  if (!lut) return null;
   492→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   493→  const startPx = Math.floor(CFG.cat.noseX * W);
   494→  const px = xRatio * W;
   495→  const idx = (px - startPx) / CFG.scoring.sampleStep;
   496→  const i0 = Math.max(0, Math.floor(idx));
   497→  const i1 = Math.min(i0 + 1, lut.length - 1);
   498→  const frac = idx - Math.floor(idx);
   499→  return lut[i0] * (1 - frac) + lut[i1] * frac;
```

```
600→  for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += spacing) {
   601→    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, 0); ctx.lineTo(x, H); ctx.stroke();
   602→  }

   608→
   609→// ============================================================
   610→// スコア計算
   611→// ============================================================
   612→function calculateScore() {
   613→  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) return 0;
   614→
   615→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   616→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   617→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   618→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   619→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   620→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   621→  let totalError = 0;
   622→  let count = 0;
   623→
   624→  // スライダー影響がある3ストロークの範囲（端点を除いた中間ピクセルのみ）
   625→  const scoredStrokes = [
   626→    // 耳（上の線）: earZoneStartX ～ earZoneEndX
   627→    { startX: SB.earZoneStartX, endX: SB.earZoneEndX, getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refTopY },
   628→    // しっぽ（上の線）: tailTopStartX ～ tailEndX
   629→    { startX: SB.tailTopStartX, endX: SB.tailEndX, getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refTopY },
   630→    // 足（下の線）: feetStartX ～ feetEndX
   631→    { startX: SB.feetStartX, endX: SB.feetEndX, getY: (xr) => getBottomY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refBottomY },
   632→  ];
   633→
   634→  for (const stroke of scoredStrokes) {
   635→    const sPx = Math.floor(stroke.startX * W);
   636→    const ePx = Math.ceil(stroke.endX * W);
   637→
   638→    for (let px = sPx; px <= ePx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   639→      // 端点はスキップ（描画で固定値を使っているため）
   640→      if (px <= sPx || px >= ePx) continue;
   641→
   642→      const xr = px / W;
   643→      const playerY = stroke.getY(xr);
   644→      const refIdx = Math.round((px - startPx) / SC.sampleStep);
   645→      if (refIdx < 0 || refIdx >= stroke.ref.length) continue;
   646→      const refY = stroke.ref[refIdx];
   647→
   648→      totalError += (refY - playerY) ** 2;
   649→      count++;
   650→    }
   651→  }
   652→
   653→  if (count === 0) return 0;
   654→  const rmse = Math.sqrt(totalError / count);
   655→  const score = Math.max(0, Math.round(SC.maxScore * Math.max(0, 1 - rmse / SC.maxRmse)));
   656→  return score;
   657→}
   658→
   659→function getScoreComment(score) {
   660→  for (const entry of LANG.scoreComments) {
   661→    if (score >= entry.min) return entry.text;
   662→  }
   663→  return '';
   664→}
   665→
   666→// ============================================================
   667→// 画面遷移
   668→// ============================================================
   669→function showScreen(name) {
   670→  document.getElementById('title-screen').style.display = name === 'title' ? 'block' : 'none';
   671→  document.getElementById('game-screen').style.display = name === 'game' ? 'block' : 'none';
   672→  document.getElementById('result-screen').style.display = name === 'result' ? 'block' : 'none';
   673→}
   674→
   675→function startGame() {
   676→  gameState = 'playing';
   677→  timeLeft = CFG.timer.duration;
   678→
   679→  resetPlayer();
   680→  syncSlidersFromPlayer();
   681→  showScreen('game');
   682→  renderGame();
   683→  updateTimerDisplay();
   684→
   685→  timerInterval = setInterval(() => {
   686→    timeLeft -= CFG.timer.intervalMs / 1000;
   687→    if (timeLeft <= 0) {
   688→      timeLeft = 0;
   689→      finishGame();
   690→    }
   691→    updateTimerDisplay();
   692→  }, CFG.timer.intervalMs);
   693→}
   694→
   695→function updateTimerDisplay() {
   696→  const el = document.getElementById('timer');
   697→  el.textContent = LANG.timerFormat.replace('{time}', timeLeft.toFixed(1));
   698→  el.classList.toggle('warning', timeLeft <= CFG.timer.warningThreshold);
   699→}
```
