   737→
   738→// デバッグ用: answerParamsのフィッティング
   739→// ブラウザコンソールから debugFit() で起動
   740→// debugSetAnswer({earHeight: 90, earGap: 30, ...}) でパラメータ変更
   741→window.debugFit = function () {
   742→  const canvas = document.getElementById('game-canvas') || document.getElementById('title-canvas');
   743→  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   744→  const W = canvas.width;

   749→  drawTargetImage(ctx, 0.3);
   750→

   752→  drawCat(ctx, CFG.answerParams, 'red', 2, 0.8);
   753→

   755→  console.log('debugSetAnswer({key: value, ...}) でパラメータを変更してください');
   756→};
   757→
   758→window.debugSetAnswer = function (overrides) {
   759→  Object.assign(CFG.answerParams, overrides);
   760→  buildBaselineLUT();
   761→  window.debugFit();
   762→};
   763→
   764→// 自動フィッティング: answerParamsを最適化
   765→window.autoFit = function () {
   766→  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) { console.error('extractContours未実行'); return; }
   767→
   768→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   769→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   770→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   771→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   772→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   773→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   774→
   775→  // 現在の数式ベースラインとの誤差を計算
   776→  function calcError(params) {
   777→    let err = 0;
   778→    let count = 0;
   779→    let idx = 0;
   780→    for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   781→      const xr = px / W;
   782→      const t = (xr - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   783→      if (t < 0 || t > 1) { idx++; continue; }
   784→
   785→      // 上線: refTopY = baseline - ears - tail を期待
   786→      const ears = getEarContribution(xr, params, W);
   787→      const tail = getTailContribution(xr, params, W, H);
   788→      const feet = getFeetContribution(xr, params, W, H);
   789→
   790→      // 上線の誤差（LUTなしの直接比較）
   791→      // getTopY(数式) = backY + faceY - ears - tail
   792→      // 理想: refTopY[idx] = getTopY(answerParams)
   793→      // ここでは数式ベースラインは使わず、refTopYとの差を最小化
   794→      const backY_val = CAT.backY * H;
   795→      const noseY_val = CAT.noseY * H;
   796→      const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);
   797→      const faceY = faceT * (noseY_val - backY_val);
   798→      const mathTop = backY_val + faceY - ears - tail;
   799→
```

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:30:19.545Z)*

*📤 結果:*
```
800→      // ※自動フィッティングではLUTを使わず、直接refTopYとparamsでの曲線を比較
   801→      // refTopY = 画像の正解 → paramsでの曲線がこれに近いほど良い
   802→      err += (refTopY[idx] - mathTop) ** 2;
   803→
   804→      // 下線: LUTベースラインを使用
   805→      const botBaseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xr);
   806→      const mathBot = (botBaseline !== null ? botBaseline : CAT.bottomY * H) + feet;
   807→      err += (refBottomY[idx] - mathBot) ** 2;
   808→
   809→      count += 2;
   810→      idx++;
   811→    }
   812→    return Math.sqrt(err / count);
   813→  }
   814→
   815→  // グリッドサーチ + 局所最適化
   816→  let best = { ...CFG.answerParams };
   817→  let bestErr = calcError(best);
   818→  console.log('初期誤差:', bestErr.toFixed(2));
   819→
   820→  // 各パラメータの探索範囲
   821→  const ranges = {
   822→    earHeight: [30, 150, 5],
   823→    earGap:    [5, 60, 3],
   824→    earWidth:  [8, 50, 3],
   825→    tailHeight:[20, 150, 5],
   826→    feetAmp:   [10, 70, 3],
   827→    feetFreq:  [2.0, 8.0, 0.2],
   828→    feetPhase: [-3.14, 3.14, 0.15]
   829→  };
   830→
   831→  // 3ラウンドの反復最適化
   832→  for (let round = 0; round < 3; round++) {
   833→    for (const [key, [min, max, step]] of Object.entries(ranges)) {
   834→      let localBest = best[key];
   835→      let localBestErr = bestErr;
   836→      const s = step / (round + 1); // ラウンドごとにステップを細かく
   837→      for (let v = min; v <= max; v += s) {
   838→        const trial = { ...best, [key]: v };
   839→        const e = calcError(trial);
   840→        if (e < localBestErr) {
   841→          localBestErr = e;
   842→          localBest = v;
   843→        }
   844→      }
   845→      best[key] = localBest;
   846→      bestErr = localBestErr;
   847→    }
   848→    console.log(`ラウンド${round + 1} 誤差: ${bestErr.toFixed(2)}`);
   849→  }
   850→
   851→  // 小数点を丸める
   852→  for (const key of Object.keys(ranges)) {
   853→    best[key] = Math.round(best[key] * 100) / 100;
   854→  }
   855→
   856→  console.log('最適化結果 answerParams:', JSON.stringify(best, null, 2));
   857→  console.log('最終誤差:', calcError(best).toFixed(2));
   858→  console.log('適用するには: debugSetAnswer(' + JSON.stringify(best) + ')');
   859→  return best;
   860→};
   861→
   862→init();
   863→
```

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:31:00.048Z)*

*🔧 ツール実行: `Edit`*
```
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "c:\\dev\\nekoegaku\\js\\game.js",
  "old_string": "// プレイヤーパラメータ",
  "new_string": "// ============================================================\n// 静的パスの読み込みとスプライン補間\n// ============================================================\nasync function loadCatPath() {\n  const res = await fetch('config/cat-path.json');\n  catPath = await res.json();\n}\n\nfunction getScaledTanY(points, i) {\n  const p = points[i];\n  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) return p.ty;\n  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];\n  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];\n  return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;\n}\n\nfunction splineY(points, xRatio) {\n  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;\n  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;\n  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;\n  let seg = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }\n  }\n  const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];\n  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;\n  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;\n  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;\n  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);\n  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);\n  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;\n  return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0\n       + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;\n}\n\nfunction buildRefFromPath() {\n  if (!catPath) return;\n  const W = CFG.canvas.width;\n  const H = CFG.canvas.height;\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const SC = CFG.scoring;\n  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);\n  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;\n\n  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n\n  let idx = 0;\n  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n    const xr = px / W;\n    refTopY[idx] = splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H;\n    refBottomY[idx] = splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xr) * H;\n    idx++;\n  }\n}\n\n// プレイヤーパラメータ"
}
```

{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "c:\\dev\\nekoegaku\\js\\game.js",
  "old_string": "// ============================================================\n// 画像から輪郭を抽出（スコア計算用）\n// ============================================================\nfunction extractContours() {\n  const W = CFG.canvas.width;\n  const H = CFG.canvas.height;\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const SC = CFG.scoring;\n  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;\n\n  const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');\n  offscreen.width = W;\n  offscreen.height = H;\n  const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');\n  drawTargetImage(octx, 1.0);\n\n  const imageData = octx.getImageData(0, 0, W, H);\n  const pixels = imageData.data;\n\n  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);\n  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;\n\n  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n\n  let idx = 0;\n  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n    let topOuter = -1;\n    let topInner = -1;\n    let bottomOuter = -1;\n    let bottomInner = -1;\n\n    // 上の線：外端（上端）を見つけてから、線の内端（下端）を探す\n    for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > SC.alphaThreshold) {\n        topOuter = y;\n        // 線の内端（最初の透明ピクセル）を探す\n        for (let y2 = y + 1; y2 < H; y2++) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= SC.alphaThreshold) {\n            topInner = y2 - 1;\n            break;\n          }\n        }\n        if (topInner === -1) topInner = topOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 下の線：外端（下端）を見つけてから、線の内端（上端）を探す\n    for (let y = H - 1; y >= 0; y--) {\n      if (pixels[(y * W + px) * 4 + 3] > SC.alphaThreshold) {\n        bottomOuter = y;\n        // 線の内端（最初の透明ピクセル）を探す\n        const xr_bottom = px / W;\n        const nearFeetEnd = xr_bottom >= SB.feetEndX - 0.02;\n        const nearFeetStart = xr_bottom <= SB.feetStartX + 0.00;\n        const maxLineSearch = (nearFeetEnd || nearFeetStart)\n          ? CFG.drawing.playerLineWidth * 3 : H;\n        for (let y2 = y - 1; y2 >= Math.max(0, y - maxLineSearch); y2--) {\n          if (pixels[(y2 * W + px) * 4 + 3] <= SC.alphaThreshold) {\n            bottomInner = y2 + 1;\n            break;\n          }\n        }\n        if (bottomInner === -1) bottomInner = bottomOuter;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 線の中央を基準にする\n    let topFound = topOuter !== -1 ? (topOuter + topInner) / 2 : -1;\n    let bottomFound = bottomOuter !== -1 ? (bottomOuter + bottomInner) / 2 : -1;\n\n    if (topFound === -1) topFound = idx > 0 ? refTopY[idx - 1] : CAT.backY * H;\n    if (bottomFound === -1) bottomFound = idx > 0 ? refBottomY[idx - 1] : CAT.bottomY * H;\n\n    refTopY[idx] = topFound;\n    refBottomY[idx] = bottomFound;\n    idx++;\n  }\n\n  smoothContour(refTopY, SC.smoothingRadius);\n  smoothContour(refBottomY, SC.smoothingRadius);\n\n  // デバッグ: refBottomYの左端付近の値を出力\n  const feetStartPx = Math.floor(SB.feetStartX * W);\n  console.log('=== refBottomY 左端付近 (feetStartX=' + SB.feetStartX + ', px=' + feetStartPx + ') ===');\n  for (let px = feetStartPx - 10; px <= feetStartPx + 40; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n    const i = Math.floor((px - startPx) / SC.sampleStep);\n    if (i >= 0 && i < refBottomY.length) {\n      const actualPx = startPx + i * SC.sampleStep;\n      const xr = actualPx / W;\n      console.log('px=' + actualPx + ' xr=' + xr.toFixed(4) + ' refBottomY=' + refBottomY[i].toFixed(1));\n    }\n  }\n\n}\n\nfunction smoothContour(arr, radius) {\n  const copy = new Float64Array(arr);\n  for (let i = radius; i < arr.length - radius; i++) {\n    let sum = 0;\n    for (let j = -radius; j <= radius; j++) sum += copy[i + j];\n    arr[i] = sum / (radius * 2 + 1);\n  }\n}",
  "new_string": ""
}

  "replace_all": false,

  "old_string": "// 自動フィッティング: answerParamsを最適化\nwindow.autoFit = function () {\n  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) { console.error('extractContours未実行'); return; }\n\n  const W = CFG.canvas.width;\n  const H = CFG.canvas.height;\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const SC = CFG.scoring;\n  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);\n\n  // 現在の数式ベースラインとの誤差を計算\n  function calcError(params) {\n    let err = 0;\n    let count = 0;\n    let idx = 0;\n    for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n      const xr = px / W;\n      const t = (xr - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);\n      if (t < 0 || t > 1) { idx++; continue; }\n\n      // 上線: refTopY = baseline - ears - tail を期待\n      const ears = getEarContribution(xr, params, W);\n      const tail = getTailContribution(xr, params, W, H);\n      const feet = getFeetContribution(xr, params, W, H);\n\n      // 上線の誤差（LUTなしの直接比較）\n      // getTopY(数式) = backY + faceY - ears - tail\n      // 理想: refTopY[idx] = getTopY(answerParams)\n      // ここでは数式ベースラインは使わず、refTopYとの差を最小化\n      const backY_val = CAT.backY * H;\n      const noseY_val = CAT.noseY * H;\n      const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);\n      const faceY = faceT * (noseY_val - backY_val);\n      const mathTop = backY_val + faceY - ears - tail;\n      // ※自動フィッティングではLUTを使わず、直接refTopYとparamsでの曲線を比較\n      // refTopY = 画像の正解 → paramsでの曲線がこれに近いほど良い\n      err += (refTopY[idx] - mathTop) ** 2;\n\n      // 下線: LUTベースラインを使用\n      const botBaseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xr);\n      const mathBot = (botBaseline !== null ? botBaseline : CAT.bottomY * H) + feet;\n      err += (refBottomY[idx] - mathBot) ** 2;\n\n      count += 2;\n      idx++;\n    }\n    return Math.sqrt(err / count);\n  }\n\n  // グリッドサーチ + 局所最適化\n  let best = { ...CFG.answerParams };\n  let bestErr = calcError(best);\n  console.log('初期誤差:', bestErr.toFixed(2));\n\n  // 各パラメータの探索範囲\n  const ranges = {\n    earHeight: [30, 150, 5],\n    earGap:    [5, 60, 3],\n    earWidth:  [8, 50, 3],\n    tailHeight:[20, 150, 5],\n    feetAmp:   [10, 70, 3],\n    feetFreq:  [2.0, 8.0, 0.2],\n    feetPhase: [-3.14, 3.14, 0.15]\n  };\n\n  // 3ラウンドの反復最適化\n  for (let round = 0; round < 3; round++) {\n    for (const [key, [min, max, step]] of Object.entries(ranges)) {\n      let localBest = best[key];\n      let localBestErr = bestErr;\n      const s = step / (round + 1); // ラウンドごとにステップを細かく\n      for (let v = min; v <= max; v += s) {\n        const trial = { ...best, [key]: v };\n        const e = calcError(trial);\n        if (e < localBestErr) {\n          localBestErr = e;\n          localBest = v;\n        }\n      }\n      best[key] = localBest;\n      bestErr = localBestErr;\n    }\n    console.log(`ラウンド${round + 1} 誤差: ${bestErr.toFixed(2)}`);\n  }\n\n  // 小数点を丸める\n  for (const key of Object.keys(ranges)) {\n    best[key] = Math.round(best[key] * 100) / 100;\n  }\n\n  console.log('最適化結果 answerParams:', JSON.stringify(best, null, 2));\n  console.log('最終誤差:', calcError(best).toFixed(2));\n  console.log('適用するには: debugSetAnswer(' + JSON.stringify(best) + ')');\n  return best;\n};",

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T09:32:17.179Z)*

*📤 結果:*
```
<tool_use_error>String to replace not found in file.
String: // 自動フィッティング: answerParamsを最適化
window.autoFit = function () {
  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) { console.error('extractContours未実行'); return; }

  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
  const CAT = CFG.cat;
  const SC = CFG.scoring;
  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);

  // 現在の数式ベースラインとの誤差を計算
  function calcError(params) {
    let err = 0;
    let count = 0;
    let idx = 0;
    for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
      const xr = px / W;
      const t = (xr - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
      if (t < 0 || t > 1) { idx++; continue; }

      // 上線: refTopY = baseline - ears - tail を期待
      const ears = getEarContribution(xr, params, W);
      const tail = getTailContribution(xr, params, W, H);
      const feet = getFeetContribution(xr, params, W, H);

      // 上線の誤差（LUTなしの直接比較）
      // getTopY(数式) = backY + faceY - ears - tail
      // 理想: refTopY[idx] = getTopY(answerParams)
      // ここでは数式ベースラインは使わず、refTopYとの差を最小化
      const backY_val = CAT.backY * H;
      const noseY_val = CAT.noseY * H;
      const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);
      const faceY = faceT * (noseY_val - backY_val);
      const mathTop = backY_val + faceY - ears - tail;
      // ※自動フィッティングではLUTを使わず、直接refTopYとparamsでの曲線を比較
      // refTopY = 画像の正解 → paramsでの曲線がこれに近いほど良い
      err += (refTopY[idx] - mathTop) ** 2;

      // 下線: LUTベースラインを使用
      const botBaseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xr);
      const mathBot = (botBaseline !== null ? botBaseline : CAT.bottomY * H) + feet;
      err += (refBottomY[idx] - mathBot) ** 2;

      count += 2;
      idx++;
    }
    return Math.sqrt(err / count);
  }

  // グリッドサーチ + 局所最適化
  let best = { ...CFG.answerParams };
  let bestErr = calcError(best);
  console.log('初期誤差:', bestErr.toFixed(2));

  // 各パラメータの探索範囲
  const ranges = {
    earHeight: [30, 150, 5],
    earGap:    [5, 60, 3],
    earWidth:  [8, 50, 3],
    tailHeight:[20, 150, 5],
    feetAmp:   [10, 70, 3],
    feetFreq:  [2.0, 8.0, 0.2],
    feetPhase: [-3.14, 3.14, 0.15]
  };

  // 3ラウンドの反復最適化
  for (let round = 0; round < 3; round++) {
    for (const [key, [min, max, step]] of Object.entries(ranges)) {
      let localBest = best[key];
      let localBestErr = bestErr;
      const s = step / (round + 1); // ラウンドごとにステップを細かく
      for (let v = min; v <= max; v += s) {
        const trial = { ...best, [key]: v };
        const e = calcError(trial);
        if (e < localBestErr) {
          localBestErr = e;
          localBest = v;
        }
      }
      best[key] = localBest;
      bestErr = localBestErr;
    }
    console.log(`ラウンド${round + 1} 誤差: ${bestErr.toFixed(2)}`);
  }

  // 小数点を丸める
  for (const key of Object.keys(ranges)) {
    best[key] = Math.round(best[key] * 100) / 100;
  }

  console.log('最適化結果 answerParams:', JSON.stringify(best, null, 2));
  console.log('最終誤差:', calcError(best).toFixed(2));
  console.log('適用するには: debugSetAnswer(' + JSON.stringify(best) + ')');
  return best;
};</tool_use_error>
```

   743→      // ※自動フィッティングではLUTを使わず、直接refTopYとparamsでの曲線を比較
   744→      // refTopY = 画像の正解 → paramsでの曲線がこれに近いほど良い
   745→      err += (refTopY[idx] - mathTop) ** 2;
   746→
   747→      // 下線: LUTベースラインを使用
   748→      const botBaseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xr);
   749→      const mathBot = (botBaseline !== null ? botBaseline : CAT.bottomY * H) + feet;
   750→      err += (refBottomY[idx] - mathBot) ** 2;
   751→
   752→      count += 2;
   753→      idx++;
   754→    }
   755→    return Math.sqrt(err / count);
   756→  }
   757→
   758→  // グリッドサーチ + 局所最適化
   759→  let best = { ...CFG.answerParams };
   760→  let bestErr = calcError(best);
   761→  console.log('初期誤差:', bestErr.toFixed(2));
   762→
   763→  // 各パラメータの探索範囲
   764→  const ranges = {
   765→    earHeight: [30, 150, 5],
   766→    earGap:    [5, 60, 3],
   767→    earWidth:  [8, 50, 3],
   768→    tailHeight:[20, 150, 5],
   769→    feetAmp:   [10, 70, 3],
   770→    feetFreq:  [2.0, 8.0, 0.2],
   771→    feetPhase: [-3.14, 3.14, 0.15]
   772→  };
   773→
   774→  // 3ラウンドの反復最適化
   775→  for (let round = 0; round < 3; round++) {
   776→    for (const [key, [min, max, step]] of Object.entries(ranges)) {
   777→      let localBest = best[key];
   778→      let localBestErr = bestErr;
   779→      const s = step / (round + 1); // ラウンドごとにステップを細かく
   780→      for (let v = min; v <= max; v += s) {
   781→        const trial = { ...best, [key]: v };
   782→        const e = calcError(trial);
   783→        if (e < localBestErr) {
   784→          localBestErr = e;
   785→          localBest = v;
   786→        }
   787→      }
   788→      best[key] = localBest;
   789→      bestErr = localBestErr;
   790→    }
   791→    console.log(`ラウンド${round + 1} 誤差: ${bestErr.toFixed(2)}`);
   792→  }
   793→
   794→  // 小数点を丸める
   795→  for (const key of Object.keys(ranges)) {
   796→    best[key] = Math.round(best[key] * 100) / 100;
   797→  }
   798→
   799→  console.log('最適化結果 answerParams:', JSON.stringify(best, null, 2));
   800→  console.log('最終誤差:', calcError(best).toFixed(2));
   801→  console.log('適用するには: debugSetAnswer(' + JSON.stringify(best) + ')');
   802→  return best;
   803→};
   804→
   805→init();
   806→
```

```
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "c:\\dev\\nekoegaku\\js\\game.js",
  "old_string": "// 自動フィッティング: answerParamsを最適化\nwindow.autoFit = function () {\n  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) { console.error('extractContours未実行'); return; }\n\n  const W = CFG.canvas.width;\n  const H = CFG.canvas.height;\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const SC = CFG.scoring;\n  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);\n\n  // 現在の数式ベースラインとの誤差を計算\n  function calcError(params) {\n    let err = 0;\n    let count = 0;\n    let idx = 0;\n    for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n      const xr = px / W;\n      const t = (xr - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);\n      if (t < 0 || t > 1) { idx++; continue; }\n\n      // 上線: refTopY = baseline - ears - tail を期待\n      const ears = getEarContribution(xr, params, W);\n      const tail = getTailContribution(xr, params, W, H);\n      const feet = getFeetContribution(xr, params, W, H);\n\n      // 上線の誤差（LUTなしの直接比較）\n      // getTopY(数式) = backY + faceY - ears - tail\n      // 理想: refTopY[idx] = getTopY(answerParams)\n      // ここでは数式ベースラインは使わず、refTopYとの差を最小化\n      const backY_val = CAT.backY * H;\n      const noseY_val = CAT.noseY * H;\n      const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);\n      const faceY = faceT * (noseY_val - backY_val);\n      const mathTop = backY_val + faceY - ears - tail;\n\n      // ※自動フィッティングではLUTを使わず、直接refTopYとparamsでの曲線を比較\n      // refTopY = 画像の正解 → paramsでの曲線がこれに近いほど良い\n      err += (refTopY[idx] - mathTop) ** 2;\n\n      // 下線: LUTベースラインを使用\n      const botBaseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xr);\n      const mathBot = (botBaseline !== null ? botBaseline : CAT.bottomY * H) + feet;\n      err += (refBottomY[idx] - mathBot) ** 2;\n\n      count += 2;\n      idx++;\n    }\n    return Math.sqrt(err / count);\n  }\n\n  // グリッドサーチ + 局所最適化\n  let best = { ...CFG.answerParams };\n  let bestErr = calcError(best);\n  console.log('初期誤差:', bestErr.toFixed(2));\n\n  // 各パラメータの探索範囲\n  const ranges = {\n    earHeight: [30, 150, 5],\n    earGap:    [5, 60, 3],\n    earWidth:  [8, 50, 3],\n    tailHeight:[20, 150, 5],\n    feetAmp:   [10, 70, 3],\n    feetFreq:  [2.0, 8.0, 0.2],\n    feetPhase: [-3.14, 3.14, 0.15]\n  };\n\n  // 3ラウンドの反復最適化\n  for (let round = 0; round < 3; round++) {\n    for (const [key, [min, max, step]] of Object.entries(ranges)) {\n      let localBest = best[key];\n      let localBestErr = bestErr;\n      const s = step / (round + 1); // ラウンドごとにステップを細かく\n      for (let v = min; v <= max; v += s) {\n        const trial = { ...best, [key]: v };\n        const e = calcError(trial);\n        if (e < localBestErr) {\n          localBestErr = e;\n          localBest = v;\n        }\n      }\n      best[key] = localBest;\n      bestErr = localBestErr;\n    }\n    console.log(`ラウンド${round + 1} 誤差: ${bestErr.toFixed(2)}`);\n  }\n\n  // 小数点を丸める\n  for (const key of Object.keys(ranges)) {\n    best[key] = Math.round(best[key] * 100) / 100;\n  }\n\n  console.log('最適化結果 answerParams:', JSON.stringify(best, null, 2));\n  console.log('最終誤差:', calcError(best).toFixed(2));\n  console.log('適用するには: debugSetAnswer(' + JSON.stringify(best) + ')');\n  return best;\n};\n\ninit();",
  "new_string": "init();"

    64→    tailImg.src = 'img/tail.png';
    65→    headImg.onload = onLoad;
    66→    tailImg.onload = onLoad;
    67→  });
    68→}
    69→
    70→// ============================================================
    71→// 静的パスの読み込みとスプライン補間
    72→// ============================================================
    73→async function loadCatPath() {
    74→  const res = await fetch('config/cat-path.json');
    75→  catPath = await res.json();
    76→}
    77→
    78→function getScaledTanY(points, i) {
    79→  const p = points[i];
    80→  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) return p.ty;
    81→  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];
    82→  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];
    83→  return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;
    84→}
    85→
    86→function splineY(points, xRatio) {
    87→  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;
    88→  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;
    89→  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;
    90→  let seg = 0;
    91→  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
    92→    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }
    93→  }
    94→  const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];
    95→  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;
    96→  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;
    97→  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;
    98→  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);
    99→  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);
   100→  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;
   101→  return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0
   102→       + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;
   103→}
   104→
   105→function buildRefFromPath() {
   106→  if (!catPath) return;
   107→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   108→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   109→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   110→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   111→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   112→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   113→  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;
   114→
   115→  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   116→  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   117→
   118→  let idx = 0;
   119→  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   120→    const xr = px / W;
   121→    refTopY[idx] = splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H;
   122→    refBottomY[idx] = splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xr) * H;
```

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T09:35:30.320Z)*

問題ないです。Step 2の実装が完了しました。変更内容をまとめます：

**追加した関数:**
- `loadCatPath()` — [game.js:73](js/game.js#L73): `config/cat-path.json`を非同期読み込み
- `getScaledTanY()` — [game.js:78](js/game.js#L78): Hermiteスプラインの接線計算（カスタムtx/ty対応）
- `splineY()` — [game.js:86](js/game.js#L86): Hermiteスプライン補間でxRatioからyRatio(0-1)を返す
- `buildRefFromPath()` — [game.js:105](js/game.js#L105): スプラインからrefTopY/refBottomYを生成（extractContoursの代替）

**変更した箇所:**
- `init()` — `loadCatPath()`をPromise.allに追加、`extractContours()`→`buildRefFromPath()`に置換
- `debugSetAnswer()` — `buildRefFromPath()`呼び出しを追加

**削除した関数:**
- `extractContours()` — 画像ピクセルスキャン（約95行）
- `smoothContour()` — 輪郭スムージング
- `getTopYNoEars()`, `getSingleEarContribution()` — ヘルパー
- `window.autoFit()` — グリッドサーチ最適化（約95行）

既存の`getTopY()`, `getBottomY()`, `buildBaselineLUT()`, `interpolateBaseline()`はそのまま動作します。refTopY/refBottomYの供給元が画像スキャン→スプラインに変わっただけなので、ベースラインLUT構築やスコア計算のロジックはそのまま使えます。

ブラウザで動作確認してみてください。`debugFit()`をコンソールで実行すると、answerParamsの曲線と手描き画像の重ね合わせが見られます。

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T10:24:39.397Z)*

ベースラインLUT構築やスコア計算のロジックはそのまま使えます←これって冗長ではないですか？どうせ得点計算にこういう仕組みが要るからいいのか？

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T10:25:26.014Z)*

良い指摘です。実際、冗長です。

今のデータフロー：
1. `splineY()` → `refTopY/refBottomY`（サンプル配列に焼く）
2. `buildBaselineLUT()` → answerParamsの寄与を足し戻して`refTopBaseline`に焼く
3. `getTopY()` → `interpolateBaseline()`でLUT補間 → playerの寄与を引く
4. `calculateScore()` → `refTopY`と比較

スプラインは任意のxで直接評価できるので、LUTに焼く必要がありません。こう簡略化できます：

- `getTopY(xr, player)` = `splineY(topLine, xr) * H + (answerEars - playerEars) + (answerTail - playerTail)`
- `getBottomY(xr, player)` = `splineY(bottomLine, xr) * H + (playerFeet - answerFeet)`
- スコア計算も`splineY() * H`と直接比較

削除できるもの：`buildBaselineLUT`, `interpolateBaseline`, `buildRefFromPath`, `refTopBaseline`, `refBottomBaseline`, `refTopY`, `refBottomY`

やりますか？

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T10:26:21.314Z)*

じゃあやりますか～

    90→  let seg = 0;
    91→  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
    92→    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }
    93→  }
    94→  const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];
    95→  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;
    96→  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;
    97→  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;
    98→  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);
    99→  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);
   100→  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;
   101→  return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0
   102→       + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;
   103→}
   104→
   105→function buildRefFromPath() {
   106→  if (!catPath) return;
   107→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   108→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   109→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   110→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   111→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   112→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   113→  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;
   114→
   115→  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   116→  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   117→
   118→  let idx = 0;
   119→  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   120→    const xr = px / W;
   121→    refTopY[idx] = splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H;
   122→    refBottomY[idx] = splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xr) * H;
   123→    idx++;
   124→  }
   125→}
   126→
   127→// プレイヤーパラメータ
   128→const player = {};
   129→
   130→function resetPlayer() {
```

68→// ============================================================
    69→async function loadCatPath() {
    70→  const res = await fetch('config/cat-path.json');
    71→  catPath = await res.json();
    72→}
    73→
    74→function getScaledTanY(points, i) {
    75→  const p = points[i];
    76→  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) return p.ty;
    77→  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];
    78→  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];
    79→  return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;
    80→}
    81→
    82→function splineY(points, xRatio) {
    83→  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;
    84→  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;
    85→  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;
    86→  let seg = 0;
    87→  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
    88→    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }
    89→  }
    90→  const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];
    91→  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;
    92→  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;
    93→  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;
    94→  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);
    95→  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);
    96→  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;
    97→  return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0
    98→       + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;
    99→}
   100→
   101→
   102→// プレイヤーパラメータ
   103→const player = {};
   104→
   105→function resetPlayer() {
   106→  Object.assign(player, CFG.playerDefaults);
   107→}
   108→
   109→// ============================================================
   110→// 上の線のy座標を計算
   111→// ============================================================
   112→function getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   113→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   114→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   115→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return CAT.noseY * H;
   116→
   117→  // LUTベースライン（元画像から抽出した固定パス）
   118→  const baseline = interpolateBaseline(refTopBaseline, xRatio);
   119→  if (baseline !== null) {
   120→    const ears = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);
   121→    const tail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   122→    return baseline - ears - tail;
   123→  }
   124→
   125→  // フォールバック: 数式ベースライン
   126→  const backY = CAT.backY * H;
   127→  const noseY = CAT.noseY * H;
   128→  const faceT = Math.max(0, 1 - t * CFG.topLine.faceDecayRate);
   129→  const faceY = faceT * (noseY - backY);
   130→
   131→  const ears = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);
   132→  const tail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   133→
   134→  return backY + faceY - ears - tail;
   135→}
   136→
   137→// ============================================================
   138→// 下の線のy座標を計算
   139→// ============================================================
   140→function getBottomY(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   141→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   142→  const BL = CFG.bottomLine;
   143→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   144→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return CAT.noseY * H;
   145→
   146→  // LUTベースライン（元画像から抽出した固定パス）
   147→  const baseline = interpolateBaseline(refBottomBaseline, xRatio);
   148→  if (baseline !== null) {
   149→    const feet = getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   150→    return baseline + feet;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // フォールバック: LUT未構築時は平坦なベースライン
   154→  const noseY = CAT.noseY * H;
   155→  const bottomBaseY = CAT.bottomY * H;
   156→
   157→  let baseY;
   158→  if (t < BL.faceEndT) {
   159→    baseY = noseY + (bottomBaseY - noseY) * (t / BL.faceEndT);
   160→  } else {
   161→    baseY = bottomBaseY;
   162→  }
   163→
   164→  const feet = getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);
   165→  return baseY + feet;
   166→}
   167→
   168→// ============================================================
   169→// ねこを描画
   170→// ============================================================
   171→function drawCat(ctx, params, color, lineWidth, alpha) {
   172→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   173→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   174→  const SC = CFG.strokeColors;
   175→  const W = ctx.canvas.width;
   176→  const H = ctx.canvas.height;
   177→  ctx.save();
   178→  ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
   179→  ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
   180→  ctx.lineCap = 'round';
   181→  ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
   182→

   184→
   185→  // ストローク1: 顔（earZoneStartX → faceBottomEndX を3次ベジェ曲線1本で描画）
   186→  ctx.strokeStyle = SC.face;
   187→  ctx.beginPath();

### 👤 ユーザー *(2026-03-22T10:29:50.666Z)*

*📤 結果:*
```
325→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   326→  const ear1X = (CAT.earCenterX - params.earGap / W) * W;
   327→  const ear2X = (CAT.earCenterX + params.earGap / W) * W;
   328→  const x = xRatio * W;
   329→  const ear1 = params.earHeight * Math.exp(-((x - ear1X) ** 2) / (2 * params.earWidth ** 2));
   330→  const ear2 = params.earHeight * Math.exp(-((x - ear2X) ** 2) / (2 * params.earWidth ** 2));
   331→  const span = CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX;
   332→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / span;
   333→  const earStartT = (SB.earZoneStartX - CAT.noseX) / span;
   334→  const earEndT = (SB.earZoneEndX - CAT.noseX) / span;
   335→  const fadeWidth = CFG.bottomLine.fadeWidth;
   336→  const envLeft = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (t - earStartT) / fadeWidth));
   337→  const envRight = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (earEndT - t) / fadeWidth));
   338→  return (ear1 + ear2) * envLeft * envRight;
   339→}
   340→
   341→function getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   342→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   343→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   344→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return 0;
   345→  const tailStart = (CFG.strokeBounds.tailTopStartX - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);
   346→  const tailT = Math.max(0, (t - tailStart) / (1 - tailStart));
   347→  const smoothTail = tailT * tailT * (3 - 2 * tailT);
   348→  return params.tailHeight * smoothTail;
   349→}
   350→
   351→
   352→function getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) {
   353→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   354→  const BL = CFG.bottomLine;
   355→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   356→  const span = CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX;
   357→  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / span;
   358→  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return 0;
   359→  const feetStartT = (SB.feetStartX - CAT.noseX) / span - BL.fadeWidth;
   360→  const feetEndT = (SB.feetEndX - CAT.noseX) / span + BL.fadeWidth;
   361→  const feetEnvLeft = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (t - feetStartT) / BL.fadeWidth));
   362→  const feetEnvRight = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (feetEndT - t) / BL.fadeWidth));
   363→  const feetEnv = feetEnvLeft * feetEnvRight;
   364→  const wave = params.feetAmp * Math.sin(params.feetFreq * Math.PI * 2 * t + params.feetPhase);
   365→  return feetEnv * wave;
   366→}
   367→
   368→function buildBaselineLUT() {
   369→  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) return;
   370→
   371→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   372→  const H = CFG.canvas.height;
   373→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   374→  const SC = CFG.scoring;
   375→  const answer = CFG.answerParams;
   376→
   377→  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);
   378→  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);
   379→  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;
   380→
   381→  refTopBaseline = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   382→  refBottomBaseline = new Float64Array(sampleCount);
   383→
   384→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;
   385→  const SJ = CFG.strokeJunctions;
   386→
   387→  let idx = 0;
   388→  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   389→    const xr = px / W;
   390→    // 上線: baseline = refTopY + ears + tail (可変部分を足し戻す)
   391→    refTopBaseline[idx] = refTopY[idx]
   392→      + getEarContribution(xr, answer, W)
   393→      + getTailContribution(xr, answer, W, H);
   394→    // 下線: baseline = refBottomY - feet (可変部分を引き戻す)
   395→    // 足の右端以降はrefBottomYがお尻/しっぽの線を拾うため、端点値で固定
   396→    let bottomBase;
   397→    if (xr >= SB.feetEndX) {
   398→      bottomBase = SJ.feetEnd_bottomY * H;
   399→    } else {
   400→      bottomBase = refBottomY[idx]
   401→        - getFeetContribution(xr, answer, W, H);
   402→    }
   403→    refBottomBaseline[idx] = bottomBase;
   404→    idx++;
   405→  }
   406→}
   407→
   408→function interpolateBaseline(lut, xRatio) {
   409→  if (!lut) return null;
   410→  const W = CFG.canvas.width;
   411→  const startPx = Math.floor(CFG.cat.noseX * W);
   412→  const px = xRatio * W;
   413→  const idx = (px - startPx) / CFG.scoring.sampleStep;
   414→  const i0 = Math.max(0, Math.floor(idx));
   415→  const i1 = Math.min(i0 + 1, lut.length - 1);
   416→  const frac = idx - Math.floor(idx);
   417→  return lut[i0] * (1 - frac) + lut[i1] * frac;
   418→}
   419→
   420→// ============================================================
   421→// ゲーム状態
   422→// ============================================================
   423→let gameState = 'title';
   424→let timeLeft = 0;
   425→let timerInterval = null;
   426→
   427→// ============================================================
   428→// スライダー ↔ プレイヤーパラメータの同期
   429→// ============================================================
   430→const sliderKeys = ['earHeight', 'earGap', 'earWidth', 'tailHeight', 'feetAmp', 'feetFreq', 'feetPhase'];
   431→
   432→function syncSlidersFromPlayer() {
   433→  for (const key of sliderKeys) {
   434→    document.getElementById(`sl-${key}`).value = player[key];
   435→  }
   436→}
   437→
   438→function syncPlayerFromSliders() {
   439→  for (const key of sliderKeys) {
   440→    player[key] = parseFloat(document.getElementById(`sl-${key}`).value);
   441→  }
   442→}
   443→
   444→function setupSliderEvents() {
```

448→  const CAT = CFG.cat;
   449→  const SB = CFG.strokeBounds;

   453→  let count = 0;
   454→
   455→  // スライダー影響がある3ストロークの範囲（端点を除いた中間ピクセルのみ）
   456→  const scoredStrokes = [
   457→    // 耳（上の線）: earZoneStartX ～ earZoneEndX
   458→    { startX: SB.earZoneStartX, endX: SB.earZoneEndX, getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refTopY },
   459→    // しっぽ（上の線）: tailTopStartX ～ tailEndX
   460→    { startX: SB.tailTopStartX, endX: SB.tailEndX, getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refTopY },
   461→    // 足（下の線）: feetStartX ～ feetEndX
   462→    { startX: SB.feetStartX, endX: SB.feetEndX, getY: (xr) => getBottomY(xr, player, W, H), ref: refBottomY },
   463→  ];
   464→
   465→  for (const stroke of scoredStrokes) {
   466→    const sPx = Math.floor(stroke.startX * W);
   467→    const ePx = Math.ceil(stroke.endX * W);
   468→
   469→    for (let px = sPx; px <= ePx; px += SC.sampleStep) {
   470→      // 端点はスキップ（描画で固定値を使っているため）
   471→      if (px <= sPx || px >= ePx) continue;
   472→
   473→      const xr = px / W;
   474→      const playerY = stroke.getY(xr);
   475→      const refIdx = Math.round((px - startPx) / SC.sampleStep);
   476→      if (refIdx < 0 || refIdx >= stroke.ref.length) continue;
   477→      const refY = stroke.ref[refIdx];
   478→
   479→      totalError += (refY - playerY) ** 2;
   480→      count++;
   481→    }
   482→  }
   483→
   484→  if (count === 0) return 0;
   485→  const rmse = Math.sqrt(totalError / count);
   486→  const score = Math.max(0, Math.round(SC.maxScore * Math.max(0, 1 - rmse / SC.maxRmse)));
   487→  return score;
```

### 🤖 Claude *(2026-03-22T10:32:27.283Z)*

不要な参照は全て消えています。862行 → 587行になりました。

**変更まとめ:**

- `getTopY()` — スプラインを直接評価し、answerParams vs playerParams の差分だけ加減算
- `getBottomY()` — 同上
- `calculateScore()` — `splineY()` を直接呼んで正解値を取得、LUT配列不要に
- **削除:** `refTopY`, `refBottomY`, `refTopBaseline`, `refBottomBaseline`（グローバル変数4つ）、`buildRefFromPath()`, `buildBaselineLUT()`, `interpolateBaseline()`, `extractContours()`, `smoothContour()`, `autoFit()`, `getTopYNoEars()`, `getSingleEarContribution()`

ロジック上、answerParamsと同じスライダー値なら `deltaEars = 0`, `deltaTail = 0`, `deltaFeet = 0` → `getTopY = splineY * H` = 正解パスそのもの → スコア100点になります。

ブラウザで動作確認してみてください。

Update debugFit/debugSetAnswer for new engine\n\n#### 実行した変更:\n\n**1. グローバル変数追加**\n```javascript\nlet catPath = null;\n```\n（refTopY等の後に追加）\n\n**2. 新関数追加（loadImages()の後に挿入）**\n```javascript\n// ============================================================\n// 静的パスの読み込みとスプライン補間\n// ============================================================\nasync function loadCatPath() {\n  const res = await fetch('config/cat-path.json');\n  catPath = await res.json();\n}\n\nfunction getScaledTanY(points, i) {\n  const p = points[i];\n  if (p.tx !== undefined && p.ty !== undefined) return p.ty;\n  const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];\n  const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];\n  return (next.y - prev.y) / 2;\n}\n\nfunction splineY(points, xRatio) {\n  if (!points || points.length < 2) return null;\n  if (xRatio <= points[0].x) return points[0].y;\n  if (xRatio >= points[points.length - 1].x) return points[points.length - 1].y;\n  let seg = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < points.length - 1; i++) {\n    if (xRatio >= points[i].x && xRatio <= points[i + 1].x) { seg = i; break; }\n  }\n  const p0 = points[seg], p1 = points[seg + 1];\n  const segLen = p1.x - p0.x;\n  if (segLen === 0) return p0.y;\n  const t = (xRatio - p0.x) / segLen;\n  const tanY0 = getScaledTanY(points, seg);\n  const tanY1 = getScaledTanY(points, seg + 1);\n  const t2 = t * t, t3 = t2 * t;\n  return (2*t3 - 3*t2 + 1) * p0.y + (t3 - 2*t2 + t) * tanY0\n       + (-2*t3 + 3*t2) * p1.y + (t3 - t2) * tanY1;\n}\n\nfunction buildRefFromPath() {\n  if (!catPath) return;\n  const W = CFG.canvas.width;\n  const H = CFG.canvas.height;\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const SC = CFG.scoring;\n  const startPx = Math.floor(CAT.noseX * W);\n  const endPx = Math.ceil(CAT.tailX * W);\n  const sampleCount = Math.floor((endPx - startPx) / SC.sampleStep) + 1;\n\n  refTopY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n  refBottomY = new Float64Array(sampleCount);\n\n  let idx = 0;\n  for (let px = startPx; px <= endPx; px += SC.sampleStep) {\n    const xr = px / W;\n    refTopY[idx] = splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H;\n    refBottomY[idx] = splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xr) * H;\n    idx++;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**3. init()修正**\n```javascript\n// Before:\nawait Promise.all([loadConfig(), loadLang(), loadImages()]);\nextractContours();\nbuildBaselineLUT();\n\n// After:\nawait Promise.all([loadConfig(), loadLang(), loadImages(), loadCatPath()]);\nbuildRefFromPath();\nbuildBaselineLUT();\n```\n\n**4. 削除した関数:**\n- `extractContours()` (L289-383, 約95行) - 画像ピクセルスキャン\n- `smoothContour()` (L385-392) - 輪郭スムージング\n- `getTopYNoEars()` (L425-427) - ヘルパー\n- `getSingleEarContribution()` (L429-432) - ヘルパー\n- `window.autoFit()` (L765-860, 約95行) - グリッドサーチ最適化\n\n**5. debugSetAnswer修正**\n```javascript\n// Before:\nwindow.debugSetAnswer = function (overrides) {\n  Object.assign(CFG.answerParams, overrides);\n  buildBaselineLUT();\n  window.debugFit();\n};\n\n// After:\nwindow.debugSetAnswer = function (overrides) {\n  Object.assign(CFG.answerParams, overrides);\n  buildRefFromPath();\n  buildBaselineLUT();\n  window.debugFit();\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n### ユーザー: LUT層の冗長性指摘\n\n> ベースラインLUT構築やスコア計算のロジックはそのまま使えます←これって冗長ではないですか？どうせ得点計算にこういう仕組みが要るからいいのか？\n\n### Claude: 冗長であると回答\n\nデータフローを分析：\n1. `splineY()` → `refTopY/refBottomY`（サンプル配列に焼く）\n2. `buildBaselineLUT()` → answerParamsの寄与を足し戻して`refTopBaseline`に焼く\n3. `getTopY()` → `interpolateBaseline()`でLUT補間 → playerの寄与を引く\n4. `calculateScore()` → `refTopY`と比較\n\nスプラインは任意のxで直接評価できるのでLUT不要。簡略化案：\n- `getTopY(xr, player)` = `splineY(topLine, xr) * H + (answerEars - playerEars) + (answerTail - playerTail)`\n- `getBottomY(xr, player)` = `splineY(bottomLine, xr) * H + (playerFeet - answerFeet)`\n- スコア計算も`splineY() * H`と直接比較\n\n削除可能: `buildBaselineLUT`, `interpolateBaseline`, `buildRefFromPath`, `refTopBaseline`, `refBottomBaseline`, `refTopY`, `refBottomY`\n\n---\n\n### ユーザー: 「じゃあやりますか〜」\n\n### Claude: LUT層の完全除去を実行\n\n#### タスクリスト:\n1. Remove refTopY/refBottomY/refTopBaseline/refBottomBaseline globals and buildRefFromPath\n2. Rewrite getTopY to use splineY directly\n3. Rewrite getBottomY to use splineY directly\n4. Remove buildBaselineLUT, interpolateBaseline\n5. Simplify calculateScore to use splineY directly\n6. Update init() and debugSetAnswer()\n\n#### 実行した変更:\n\n**1. グローバル変数削除**\n```javascript\n// 削除:\nlet refTopY = null;\nlet refBottomY = null;\nlet refTopBaseline = null;\nlet refBottomBaseline = null;\n\n// 残す:\nlet catPath = null;\n```\n\n**2. buildRefFromPath()削除**\n（前のステップで追加したばかりだが、冗長なので即削除）\n\n**3. getTopY書き換え**\n```javascript\n// Before (LUT経由):\nfunction getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H) {\n  const CAT = CFG.cat;\n  const t = (xRatio - CAT.noseX) / (CAT.tailX - CAT.noseX);\n  if (t < 0 || t > 1) return CAT.noseY * H;\n  const baseline = interpolateBaseline(refTopBaseline, xRatio);\n  if (baseline !== null) {\n    const ears = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W);\n    const tail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H);\n    return baseline - ears - tail;\n  }\n  // フォールバック...\n}\n\n// After (splineY直接):\nfunction getTopY(xRatio, params, W, H) {\n  if (!catPath) return CFG.cat.noseY * H;\n  const answer = CFG.answerParams;\n  const base = splineY(catPath.topLine, xRatio) * H;\n  const deltaEars = getEarContribution(xRatio, params, W) - getEarContribution(xRatio, answer, W);\n  const deltaTail = getTailContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) - getTailContribution(xRatio, answer, W, H);\n  return base - deltaEars - deltaTail;\n}\n```\n\n**4. getBottomY書き換え**\n```javascript\n// After:\nfunction getBottomY(xRatio, params, W, H) {\n  if (!catPath) return CFG.cat.noseY * H;\n  const answer = CFG.answerParams;\n  const base = splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xRatio) * H;\n  const deltaFeet = getFeetContribution(xRatio, params, W, H) - getFeetContribution(xRatio, answer, W, H);\n  return base + deltaFeet;\n}\n```\n\n**5. buildBaselineLUT, interpolateBaseline削除**\n（約50行を削除）\n\n**6. calculateScore書き換え**\n```javascript\n// Before:\nfunction calculateScore() {\n  if (!refTopY || !refBottomY) return 0;\n  // ...refTopY配列からインデックスで参照...\n}\n\n// After:\nfunction calculateScore() {\n  if (!catPath) return 0;\n  const scoredStrokes = [\n    { startX: SB.earZoneStartX, endX: SB.earZoneEndX,\n      getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H),\n      refY: (xr) => splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H },\n    { startX: SB.tailTopStartX, endX: SB.tailEndX,\n      getY: (xr) => getTopY(xr, player, W, H),\n      refY: (xr) => splineY(catPath.topLine, xr) * H },\n    { startX: SB.feetStartX, endX: SB.feetEndX,\n      getY: (xr) => getBottomY(xr, player, W, H),\n      refY: (xr) => splineY(catPath.bottomLine, xr) * H },\n  ];\n  // ...refY(xr)で直接スプライン評価...\n}\n```\n\n**7. init()修正**\n```javascript\n// Before:\nbuildRefFromPath();\nbuildBaselineLUT();\n\n// After:\n// （両方削除、loadCatPathはPromise.allに残る）\n```\n\n**8. debugSetAnswer修正**\n```javascript\n// Before:\nwindow.debugSetAnswer = function (overrides) {\n  Object.assign(CFG.answerParams, overrides);\n  buildRefFromPath();\n  buildBaselineLUT();\n  window.debugFit();\n};\n\n// After:\nwindow.debugSetAnswer = function (overrides) {\n  Object.assign(CFG.answerParams, overrides);\n  window.debugFit();\n};\n```\n\n#### 最終確認:\n- `grep`で旧変数・関数名の残存チェック → 0件\n- 862行 → 587行（275行削減）\n\n---\n\n### ユーザー: 「このセッションの会話を省略・要約せずにそのままlogsに書き出して」\n\n---\n\n## 削除された関数・変数の一覧\n\n### グローバル変数（削除）\n- `refTopY` - 正解上線のY座標サンプル配列\n- `refBottomY` - 正解下線のY座標サンプル配列\n- `refTopBaseline` - 上線ベースラインLUT\n- `refBottomBaseline` - 下線ベースラインLUT\n\n### 関数（削除）\n- `extractContours()` - 画像ピクセルスキャンで輪郭抽出\n- `smoothContour()` - 移動平均によるスムージング\n- `buildBaselineLUT()` - answerParamsの寄与を除去したベースラインLUT構築\n- `interpolateBaseline()` - LUTの線形補間\n- `buildRefFromPath()` - スプラインからrefTopY/refBottomY生成（追加後すぐ削除）\n- `getTopYNoEars()` - 耳なしの上線Y座標\n- `getSingleEarContribution()` - 単一耳のガウシアン寄与\n- `window.autoFit()` - グリッドサーチによるanswerParams最適化\n\n### 関数（書き換え）\n- `getTopY()` - LUT参照 → splineY直接評価 + delta方式\n- `getBottomY()` - LUT参照 → splineY直接評価 + delta方式\n- `calculateScore()` - refTopY/refBottomY配列参照 → splineY直接評価\n- `init()` - extractContours/buildBaselineLUT呼び出し削除、loadCatPath追加\n- `debugSetAnswer()` - buildRefFromPath/buildBaselineLUT呼び出し削除\n\n### 関数（新規追加）\n- `loadCatPath()` - cat-path.jsonの非同期読み込み\n- `getScaledTanY()` - Hermiteスプラインの接線計算\n- `splineY()` - Hermiteスプライン補間（任意のxRatioでyRatioを返す）\n\n## 現在のステータス\n- Step 1: 完了（パスエディタ+パス確定）\n- Step 2: 完了（静的パス+スプライン統合 + LUT層除去）\n- Step 3: 未着手（描画・スコア計算の更新 — ただしスコア計算は既にStep 2で更新済み）\n- Step 4: 未着手（不要コード削除・設定整理 — ただし大部分はStep 2で完了済み）\n- ブラウザでの動作確認: ユーザー未実施\n"
